Why WestJet:

Every WestJet journey has the potential to enrich lives; a career with us is no exception.

WestJet arrived on the Canadian airline scene in 1996 and changed the industry for the better. We made air travel more affordable for Canadians and now we're going global.

Join us and love where you’re going.

 Hybrid Role: 

This is a hybrid position; on occasion, you will be required to work at the WestJet Campus in Calgary approximately 2 days / week. Calgary based candidates required.

Reporting to the Director of Financial Planning and Analysis (“FP&A”), WestJet is seeking a Flight Profitability Systems Analyst to support the WestJet Group with managing the critical Flight Profitability System (“FPS”) to support Network Planning with strategic and tactical network decisions.

In order to be successful, the candidate will have to work closely alongside key stakeholders across the Group including Finance, Network Planning, Revenue Management and Fleet Planning as well as externa system support vendors and 3rd party consultants for complex issue resolutions.

Key deliverables and accountabilities include:

 Liaise with IT on all matters related to FPS ensuring data availability and capture; 
 Obtain and process raw and source data with FPS to ensure efficient running of FPS program; 
 Maintaining and updating flight profitability logic and allocation methodologies, as required; 
 FPS maintenance and continuous development and enhancement of the system; 
 Conduct thorough analysis of existing systems and processes to identify areas for improvement; 
 Perform data analysis and identify abnormalities that exceed defined thresholds; 
 Perform thorough quality assurance to ensure continued accuracy of data and information used for FPS 
 Provide analytical support, conduct research and reviews to ensure use of most appropriate data sources 
 Design, test and implement changes to account structure and hierarchy changes for financial data and allocations in Flight Profitability; 
 Design and propose innovative and effective system solutions that align with business needs; 
 Work closely with development teams to implement and deploy new systems or enhance existing ones; 
 Create detailed documentation, including system specifications, user manuals, and workflow diagrams and ensure such documentation is up-to-date and accessible to relevant stakeholders; 
 Develop and execute comprehensive test plans to ensure the reliability and performance of systems and address any issues or bugs during the testing phase; 
 Provide ongoing support and troubleshooting for existing systems, addressing issues promptly; 
 Stay abreast of emerging technologies and industry trends to recommend enhancements and upgrades; 
 Evaluate and recommend third-party solutions that align with organizational goals; and 
 Be an active member of the Finance team; willing to mentor and coach peers, brainstorm issues, and be flexible in completing any task 

Experience and qualifications: 

 Completion of a postsecondary degree in Commerce or Business Administration. A Bachelors degree in Computer Science, Information Technology or related field would be considered an asset 
 3 to 5 years of experience in progressively complex financial analysis roles 
 Experience with and ability to distill large data sets in order to determine relevant information needs 
 Strong communicator who demonstrates ability to focus communication to the needs of the audience and translate financial information to operational information 
 Attention to detail, organized and thorough, with a desire for continuous improvement 
 Ability to analyze business results, identify and clearly summarize key issues 
 Excel proficiency (ability to prepare pivot tables, VLOOKUP formulas, etc.) 
 Experience using Access databases, Oracle EPM (Hyperion), or equivalent systems 
 Experience with business intelligence tools and/or proven ability to learn new systems quickly (SQL, Alteryx, Tableau, Power BI, etc.) 
 Experience identifying requirements and testing finance modules for new software system implementation would be considered an asset 
 Experience in implementing new systems, processes and policies 
 Works independently, displaying an intellectual curiosity that can create process efficiencies and drive improvements for the team 
 Able to handle pressure and meet tight timelines in an environment with a high volume of activity 
 Ability to maintain a high level of confidentiality

 A fun and friendly culture with colleagues who work together to win 
 Travel privileges for you and your family, effective from your start date 
 Savings and Benefit programs that are flexible to meet your specific needs

About WestJet Group Of Companies

Together with WestJet's regional airline, WestJet Encore, we offer scheduled service to more than 100 destinations in North America, Central America, the Caribbean and Europe and to more than 175 destinations in over 20 countries through our airline partnerships.

Our Safety Promise 

At WestJet, the safety and security of our people and our guests is a core value and at the heart of what we do. As safety and security is a shared responsibility, it is expected that you will use safe work practices to ensure your well-being and the safety of others.

WestJet recognizes that the use of Alcohol and Drugs can adversely impact a safe work environment and the well-being of others including guests, suppliers and the public, as well as place WestJet's operations at risk. All roles that are identified as safety sensitive are required to pass a Pre-Employment Alcohol and Drug Test as per WestJet's Alcohol and Drug Policy. 

Our Commitment to Diversity and Inclusion 

We embrace what makes us each unique, and what makes us uniquely WestJet. WestJet is committed to inclusiveness, equity, and accessibility and if you require accommodation during the selection process, please let our Talent Acquisition team know. We encourage all qualified candidates to apply. We thank all applicants for their interest in WestJet; however, only those candidates who are selected will be contacted.

For more information about everything WestJet, please visit WestJet.com

Remote Data Analysis Tutor Jobs

The Varsity Tutors platform has thousands of students looking for online Data Analysis tutors nationally. As a tutor who uses the Varsity Tutors platform, you can earn good money, choose your own hours, and truly make a difference in the lives of your students.

Why join our platform?

Enjoy competitive rates and get paid 2x per week.
Choose to tutor as much or as little as you want.
Set your own hours and schedule.
Get paired with students best-suited to your teaching style and preferences (from thousands of potential clients).
Tutor online (i.e. “work remotely”) using our purpose-built Live Learning Platform.
Students can take adaptive assessments through the platform and share results to help you decide where to focus.
We collect payment from the customers, so all you have to do is invoice the session.

What We Look For In a Tutor

You have excellent communication skills and a friendly, approachable personality.
You can show subject-matter expertise in Data Analysis.
You have the ability to personalize lessons for each student.

Discover all the ways you can reach students through the online platform:

1-on-1 Online Tutoring: connect with an individual student for a highly personalized learning experience.
Small Group Classes: meet with small groups (typically 7-9 students) for a more collaborative learning experience.
Large Live Classes: share your knowledge with hundreds of students at a time.
Instant Tutoring: accept subject-specific, on-demand tutoring sessions whenever you’d like.

About Varsity Tutors And 1-on-1 Online Tutoring

Our mission is to transform the way people learn. We do this by leveraging advanced technology, AI, and the latest in learning science to facilitate a personalized learning experience. With 1-on-1 Online Tutoring, individual students are connected with tutors for a highly personalized learning experience. We believe our thoughtful approach to matching students with the right tutors can improve outcomes, and we look forward to connecting you with students hungry to learn.

Description

Position Summary

Data Analysis Trainee assists in analysis activities including data setup, data searches, feature identification and marking.
Primary Responsibilities
Safety shall always be the top priority
Work in a team environment collaborating and sharing knowledge and experiences
Learn the responsibilities and required tasks of a Level I Data Analysis.
Accomplish all requirements of a Level I Data Analysis qualification and pass respective evaluation.
Interpret industry documentation on ILI tools and pipeline integrity
Under the supervision of a Data Analysis Level II or higher perform data preparation and processing of ILI data
Under the supervision of a Data Analysis Level II or higher perform feature categorization, evaluation and marking
Performs other assigned tasks

Requirements

Degree or diploma in engineering, science or technical discipline; or equivalent experience preferred
Strong work ethic with a can-do attitude
Proficient with operating relevant customized and shrink-wrap computer software applications
Understanding of Microsoft Suite Products.
Demonstrated ability to deliver timely, accurate, and complete results
Requires a strong ability to sustain focus on one or more tasks while avoiding distractions.
Willingness to handle repetitive tasks
Requires pattern recognition and spatial thinking skill.
Must be customer focused, have an excellent attention to detail and a strong ability to work in a team environment
About the job
Inspirantes, ingénieuses, animées de l’esprit d’entreprise : voilà ce qui décrit bien nos équipes d’exception. Donnez une vocation à votre passion en rejoignant une culture qui s’épanouit face au changement.

Faites votre marque au sein du Groupe des normes professionnelles en certification - Conception des méthodes de certification à titre de directeur(trice). Cette équipe diversifiée de professionnels mise sur son expertise technique et sectorielle pour contribuer, à l’interne, au succès de notre pratique de certification et de comptabilité. En tant que conseiller de confiance, vous jouerez un rôle influent en matière de nouvelles tendances et de changements pour vous assurer que nos membres répondent aux normes les plus rigoureuses du secteur.

Notre identité canadienne est pour nous une source de fierté. Nous sommes un cabinet de comptabilité, de fiscalité et de services-conseils de premier plan au Canada qui propose des stratégies et des solutions aux entreprises. Entrepreneurs dans l’âme, les membres talentueux de notre équipe voient les obstacles comme des occasions de se dépasser et transforment les façons de faire sur le marché des petites et moyennes entreprises.

Responsabilités

Promouvoir l’importance du contrôle de la qualité auprès des associés, des directeurs et des autres membres du cabinet et jouer un rôle central dans les initiatives du cabinet visant la qualité.
Appuyer la conception et la mise à jour des politiques et des lignes directrices encadrant les missions du cabinet de même que ses protocoles de comptabilité et d’audit.
Se tenir au courant des changements dans la profession en effectuant des recherches et en prenant part à des activités et à des séances de formation organisées dans le secteur.
Contribuer à la conception et faciliter la mise en œuvre des formations en certification dans le cadre des programmes de perfectionnement interne exhaustifs de MNP.
Entretenir des liens et des échanges professionnels avec les équipes de certification et de comptabilité du cabinet et avec ses équipes de direction.
Acquérir une solide compréhension des services de MNP ainsi que des entreprises et des secteurs servis par le cabinet.
Prendre part à l’élaboration de nouvelles idées et méthodes pour améliorer les procédures de travail.
Optimiser les effectifs afin qu’un travail complet et exact soit livré dans le respect des échéances.
Fournir un mentorat aux membres de l’équipe, les motiver et les encadrer pour qu’ils puissent se perfectionner et s’épanouir grâce à des objectifs clairs, à une rétroaction régulière et à une résolution rapide des problèmes de rendement, en plus de procéder aux évaluations de rendement.
Être disposé à se déplacer, au besoin.


Compétences et expérience 

Minimum de deux ans d'expérience à titre de comptable principal(e) dans le service de certification d’un des sept grands cabinets comptables et expérience antérieure en certification
Expérience de la conception et la mise en œuvre de procédures d’audit fondées sur le risque et le caractère significatif
Capacité de communiquer et d'écrire en Français et en anglais 
Connaissance des
Contrôles internes et de leur application
Diverses normes comptables (p. ex., NCECF, NCOSBL, NCSP)
Interprétation et application des normes de certification (p. ex., NCA et/ou ISA)
Compétences en rédaction technique et en gestion de projets; compréhension des principes commerciaux, de gestion et d’expansion des affaires s’appliquant à un cabinet

MesAvantages@MNP 

Offrant un potentiel de revenus élevés, MNP est fier de proposer des avantages taillés sur mesure qui sont à l’image de notre culture d’exception et qui favorisent un mode de vie équilibré, le tout pour aider ses membres à s’épanouir, tant au bureau que dans leur vie personnelle. Vous profiterez d’un salaire de base généreux, de vacances, de quatre congés personnels payés par année, d’un régime collectif de retraite avec cotisations égalées à 4 %, de produits d’épargne volontaire, de programmes de primes, d’avantages sociaux à la carte, de ressources en santé mentale, d’un accès exclusif à des rabais et à des avantages indirects, d’une aide au perfectionnement professionnel, de cours offerts à l’interne par l’intermédiaire de MNP University, d’un code vestimentaire adapté à vos tâches, d’activités sociales organisées par le cabinet, et plus encore!

Diversité@MNP

Chez MNP, la diversité est l’une de nos valeurs de base et nous célébrons nos différences. Nous croyons que chaque membre de notre cabinet apporte ses talents uniques et que la mise en valeur de son potentiel nous rend collectivement plus forts. About the job
AN ENGLISH VERSION WILL FOLLOW 

DESCRIPTION DE L'ENTREPRISE
Castle Hall est une entreprise entrepreneuriale, dynamique et en pleine évolution qui cherche à embauché un Analyste en Contrôle Diligent & Données à son équipe de Montréal. Ce rôle répond à l'augmentation de demande pour les services de Castle Hall et à l'engagement de l'entreprise à poursuivre sa croissance.

RESPONSABILITÉS

Contrôle Diligent
Dans ce rôle capital, vous participerez à un ensemble complet de tâches visant à optimiser les processus de contrôle diligent et à servir de base à la prise de décisions judicieuses en matière d’investissement. Vos responsabilités engloberont une série d’activités importantes.
Examen approfondi des documents: examiner les principaux documents relatifs aux fonds comme les prospectus, les états financiers, les contrats et les dossiers de conformité. Votre analyse approfondie jouera un rôle important dans la compréhension globale du contexte de l’investissement.
Assurance de l’intégrité des données: assurer l’exactitude et la fiabilité des données sur les fonds et sur les gestionnaires de fonds, qui figurent dans la base de données dynamique de contrôle diligent de Castle Hall. Votre souci du détail permettra de disposer d’une base d’information fiable.
Mobilisation des gestionnaires d’actifs mondiaux: avoir des entretiens éclairants sur le contrôle diligent avec des gestionnaires d’actifs mondiaux. Votre capacité à obtenir des renseignements pertinents sera indispensable pour favoriser des choix éclairés en matière d’investissement.
Production de rapports complets: consigner habilement vos conclusions dans des rapports détaillés sur le contrôle diligent. Ces rapports, qui comprennent notamment des textes descriptifs présentés clairement et la détermination des facteurs de risque pertinents à l’aide de l’application avancée de gestion des risques de Castle Hall, serviront de références indispensables.
Définition et description des changements: demeurer à l’écoute des changements en cours dans les structures de financement et chez les gestionnaires de fonds. Votre capacité à constater, analyser et consigner rapidement ces changements sera essentielle pour avoir des informations à jour.
Collaboration avec les clients: collaborer efficacement avec les clients en leur communiquant en amont les résultats du contrôle diligent de façon claire. Vos observations joueront un rôle fondamental dans l’enrichissement du processus décisionnel de nos clients en matière d’investissement.
Entretien des relations: favoriser des relations positives et professionnelles avec les gestionnaires de fonds qui soulignent votre engagement en faveur de l’excellence et créent un environnement propice à une collaboration fructueuse.
Amélioration de la plateforme: jouer un rôle actif dans l’évolution de la plateforme OpsDiligence. Vos commentaires orienteront l’amélioration continue de la plateforme, ce qui permettra de rendre les processus de contrôle diligent encore plus efficaces.

Données
Intégrer les gestionnaires de fonds et les clients à notre plateforme OpsDiligence.
Examiner et saisir diverses données financières, comme celles relatives aux fonds de couverture et aux placements privés en titres de capitaux propres, et assurer la coordination avec certains gestionnaires de fonds et prestataires de services.
Engager des conversations téléphoniques avec des gestionnaires d’actifs mondiaux ayant diverses stratégies et tailles.
Extraire, compiler et gérer les documents reçus des gestionnaires de fonds et vérifier leur exactitude avant de les ajouter au système dorsal de traitement exclusif de Castle Hall.
Déterminer les stratégies des fonds communs de placement assujettis à une couverture en vérifiant des points de données dans des documents exclusifsde commercialisation et de gestion ainsi que dans des documents juridiques, comme les notices d’offre et les conventions de sociétés en commandite, et saisir avec exactitude les données essentielles pour le client dans le système dorsal de traitement de Castle Hall.

COMPÉTENCES ET EXPÉRIENCE SOUHAITÉES
Une licence en finance, commerce, affaires, comptabilité ou dans une discipline connexe.
Aspirer à développer une carrière dans le secteur de la diligence opérationnelle au sein de l'industrie de l'investissement alternatif.
Un souci du détail exceptionnel, associé à d'excellentes aptitudes à la communication écrite et orale en anglais.
Capacité à produire un travail de qualité sous pression et dans des délais serrés
Confiance et maturité pour transmettre les résultats de la due diligence aux investisseurs institutionnels et devenir un conseiller de confiance pour les répartiteurs d'actifs mondiaux.

CE QUE NOUS OFFRONS
Régime d'avantages sociaux comprenant une couverture des soins de la vue et des soins dentaires.
Plan d'épargne retraite avec cotisations équivalentes.
Portail de bien-être en ligne gratuit pour tous les employés.
Jours de vacances payés et jours de congés supplémentaires pour Noël et les vacances d'été.
Un compte de dépenses personnelles.
Remboursement des frais de formation et de développement pour les titres pertinents.
Jours de congé supplémentaires pour la préparation des examens.
Un plan de pension avec une contribution équivalente.

  COMPANY DESCRIPTION

Castle Hall is an entrepreneurial, dynamic and fast moving company that is looking to hire a Due Diligence & Data Analyst to our Montreal team. This role responds to increasing demand for Castle Hall’s services, and the firm’s commitment to continued growth.

RESPONSIBILITIES
Diligence:

Thorough Document Review: Dive into key fund documents, such as prospectuses, financial statements, contracts, and compliance records. Your insightful analysis will be instrumental in forming a comprehensive understanding of the investment landscape.
Data Integrity Assurance: Assure the accuracy and reliability of fund and management company data residing in Castle Hall’s dynamic due diligence database. Your meticulous approach will contribute to maintaining a robust informational foundation.
Global Asset Manager Engagement: Conduct insightful due diligence interviews with asset managers worldwide. Your adeptness at extracting relevant information will be integral in fostering informed investment choices.
Comprehensive Reporting: Skillfully document your findings in meticulous due diligence reports. These reports, complete with articulate narratives and the identification of pertinent risk factors using Castle Hall’s advanced risk management application, will serve as indispensable references.
Change Identification and Documentation: Stay attuned to ongoing changes within fund structures and management companies. Your ability to swiftly identify, analyze, and document these changes will be pivotal in maintaining up-to-the-minute insights.
Client Collaboration: Collaborate effectively with clients, conveying due diligence findings in a clear and proactive manner. Your insights will play a crucial role in enriching our clients’ investment decision-making process.
Relationship Cultivation: Foster positive and professional relationships with investment managers, underlining your commitment to excellence and creating a conducive environment for productive collaboration.
Platform Enhancement: Contribute actively to the evolution of the OpsDiligence platform. Your input will shape the platform's continuous improvement, enabling even more effective due diligence processes.
Versatile Contributions: Seamlessly tackle ad-hoc special projects and administrative tasks as needed. Your adaptability and willingness to embrace varied responsibilities will be instrumental in maintaining operational efficiency.

Data:
Onboard investment managers and clients to our OpsDiligence platform.
Review and input various financial information such as those related to hedge funds and private equity investment funds as well as coordinating with certain investment managers and service providers.
Conducting calls with global asset managers across various strategies and sizes.
Extract, compile, and manage documents received from investment managers and verify their accuracy before adding them into the back-end proprietary system of Castle Hall.
Determine the strategies of the investment funds under coverage by verifying data points across marketing and manager proprietary materials as well as legal documents such as offering memoranda, limited partnership agreements, etc. and accurately input vital information for the client into Castle Hall’s back-end system.

DESIRED SKILLS AND EXPERIENCE
A Bachelor’s degree in finance, commerce, business, accounting, or a related discipline.
Demonstrated intellectual curiosity and willingness to take on challenges in analyzing complex organizations and control environments, including accounting, operational, and valuation issues faced by asset managers.
Aspire to develop a career path in the operational due diligence sector within the alternative investment industry.
Exceptional attention to detail, combined with excellent English Written and verbal communication skills.
Ability to produce quality work under pressure and tight deadlines.
Confidence and maturity to relay due diligence findings to institutional investors and become a trusted advisor to global asset allocators.

WHAT WE OFFER
Benefits plan including vision and dental coverage.
Retirement Savings Plan with matching contributions.
Online wellness portal free to all employees.
Paid vacation days and additional bonus days off during Christmas & summer holidays.
A personal spending account.
Learning and Development reimbursements for relevant designations.
Additional days off for exam preparation.
Pension plan with matching contribution.
About the job
Summary of Duties:
Reporting to the Corporate Information Officer, the Database Administrator and Data Governance Analyst (DBA) is responsible for the maintenance, security, and efficient operation of both Oracle and SQL servers and databases. This role oversees the City's data policies, ensuring data security and governance. The DBA is involved in applying updates, generating reports, assisting with data conversions for upcoming projects, and maintaining all application databases.
This position works with the various members of the Information Technology team to create efficiencies, review current processes, analyze, and develop or modify databases including coding stored procedures, testing, debugging, and installing database software. This position provides direction and guidance on the use of the various technologies for process improvements usability and accessibility.
 Duties and Responsibilities:
(These set out the principal functions of the position, and shall not be considered as a detailed description of all the work requirements).
Develop databases for new applications which includes building development, testing, user acceptance and production databases.
Develop standards for database structures. Write technical procedures and documentation for database technology including operations, user guide, etc.
Develop database backup and recovery scripts for new databases and database environments including disaster recovery procedures.
Optimize database structures for application performance. Monitor database environment's disk & CPU usage. Ensure environments has sufficient resources.
Recommend database technology for new solutions.
Evaluate new vendor software as it relates to databases.
Participate as a member of the Records Information Management (RIM) project team. 
Apply database maintenance including patches, releases and versions to database environments and database tools.
Participate in the modeling of data in conjunction with the developers. Write conversion scripts to move data.
Design the test plan in collaboration with the Business Support Analyst.
Act as an agent of change for the corporation.
Develop and enhance data governance policies including data classification and data retention.
Act as project leader on development and maintenance projects (planning, scheduling, monitoring, and reporting).
Perform other related duties as assigned. 

Position Requirements: 
University Degree in Information Technology, Computer Science, Software Engineering or related field. 
Five (5) years database administration and data governance experience in an on-line multi-user environment within a medium sized IT Department. 
Three (3) years experience in monitoring and managing Oracle databases. 
Project Management, Lean Six Sigma, Business Analysis, or ITIL Certifications are considered an asset. 
Proven knowledge of data governance and data security including relevant data privacy regulations.
Knowledge and experience in data modeling.
Expert knowledge of and experience with ORACLE RDBMS, SQL/PLSQ, and Microsoft SOL RDBMS.
Certificates in database administration for Oracle and MS SQL server are considered an asset. 
Proficiency with Microsoft Power BI, Tableau and SSRS tools.
Knowledge of and experience with Toad software and Crystal Reports.
Expert knowledge of and experience applying software patches to RDBMS.
Ability to identify and solve database issues. 
Ability to gather and analyze user requirements and make appropriate suggestions. 
Ability to think proactively to solve support issues and prevent future occurrences. 
Good interpersonal, relationship building and communication skills. 
Proven completion of Ministry of Labour Worker Health and Safety Awareness training. 
Demonstrated commitment to a safety culture.

CUPE 157 Pay Group 11 – Minimum $82,968 annually; Maximum $95,200 annually
Expected Work Location: City Hall (eligible for remote work)
Hours of Work: Currently Monday-Friday 8:30am-4:30pm

Introduction:

ICES is currently seeking an Information Management Analyst to join our Data Quality & Information Management Department. Reporting to the Lead Specialist, the Information Management Analyst is responsible for the import and maintenance of large health services data sets in a SAS/LINUX environment under stringent confidentiality and security guidelines. The Information Management Analyst will convert the administrative data to SAS datasets, perform data cleaning and validation activities, document data characteristics, and perform routine data archiving activities and implementation of ICES data destruction policy. The Information Management Analyst will assume data management and processing responsibilities of ICES record linkage research projects. The Information Management Analyst will demonstrate a comprehensive understanding of specific ICES data holdings and ICES’ privacy, confidentiality and security policies and Guidelines.

Responsibilities of the position include, but may not be limited to:

Recode any direct personal identifiers as it arrives at ICES as the first use;
Develop and process SAS programs to convert administrative and study data files to SAS datasets;
Act as an ICES Administrative Data Covenanter;
Perform data cleaning and validation activities, documentation of data characteristics according to P&B standards and guidelines;
Perform electronic archiving of specific ICES databases;
Carry out data destruction following ICES data destruction policy;
Receive data collected in ICES primary data collection projects and prepares for the ICES research environment (LINUX);
Perform ad-hoc data transferring requests;
Communicate with Technology department, Research Program Managers, and/or Project Managers to solve data issues;
Communicate with ICES data providers as necessary;
Other duties as may be assigned within the scope of this position.

Knowledge, skills, and abilities required: 
Bachelor’s degree in computer science, Biostatistics, or related field;
3 years of related work experience;
Working knowledge of principles of computer systems architecture, database design and record linkage methodology;
Proficient in SAS programming;
Excellent understanding of the concepts of data privacy, confidentiality, and security practices;
Understanding of the LINUX operating system for data security management practices, ICES Primary Data Collection Utility and how to use administrative data in health services research is an asset;
Beginner to intermediate proficiency in other programming languages like SQL and python would be an advantage;
Good organizational skills;
Excellent oral and written communication skills.
 
This is a full-time opportunity at ICES Central. Successful candidate must reside within Ontario while working remotely and able to come into the office if required from time to time. There may be instances where in-person meetings are requested; however, ICES continues to support Flexible remote work arrangements anywhere in Ontario.

Security clearance may be required.

Interested candidates should submit their resume and cover letter detailing how their knowledge, skills and abilities match the scope of this position.

Who We Are

Geotab ® is a global leader in IoT and connected transportation and certified “Great Place to Work ™ .” We are a company of diverse and talented individuals who work together to help businesses grow and succeed, and increase the safety and sustainability of our communities.

Geotab is advancing security, connecting commercial vehicles to the internet and providing web-based analytics to help customers better manage their fleets. Geotab’s open platform and Geotab Marketplace ® , offering hundreds of third-party solution options, allows both small and large businesses to automate operations by integrating vehicle data with their other data assets. Processing billions of data points a day, Geotab leverages data analytics and machine learning to improve productivity, optimize fleets through the reduction of fuel consumption, enhance driver safety and achieve strong compliance to regulatory changes.

Who You Are

We are always looking for amazing talent who can contribute to our growth and deliver results! Geotab is seeking a Senior Data Analyst, ITS who will create compelling and original content (blogs, white papers, articles, presentations, etc.) for Geotab’s Intelligent Transportations Systems (ITS) division. If you love technology, and are keen to join an industry leader — we would love to hear from you!

What You'll Do

The Senior Data Analyst, ITS uncover trends, patterns, and insights that will focus people’s attention on the key value of Geotab ITS data. This person will be a crucial component to drive Geotab’s thought leadership related to smart cities and intelligent transportation. To be successful in this role you will be a self-starter and problem solver with strong written and verbal communication skills, and have the ability to quickly understand complex, technical concepts.

How You’ll Make An Impact

Examine large data sets to identify trends, develop charts, and create visual presentations to help businesses make more strategic decisions.
Apply statistical methods toward data validation of Geotab aggregate traffic-related data against third-party data sources
Utilize statistical tools to interpret data sets and prepare reports and technical papers that effectively communicate trends, patterns, and predictions based on relevant findings.
Write SQL queries to find answers to complex business questions.
Identify any data quality issues and partialities in data acquisition.
Coordinate with engineering teams to gather incremental new data.
Process, cleanse, and verify the integrity of data used for analysis.
Use data mining, model building, and other analytical techniques to develop customer segmentation.
Work with data scientists and leverage machine learning models that have been developed against Geotab’s big data environment.

What You’ll Bring To This Role

Post-secondary Degree/Diploma specialization in Computer Science, Software Engineering, Science, Mathematics, or a related field.
5-8 years experience as a Data Analyst or a similar role.
5-8 years experience with SQL.
5-8 years experience with data science tools (e.g. Python, Pandas, NumPy) as well as BI tools such as Superset/Redash/PowerBI or tableau.
Experience working with big data and an understanding of techniques used to extract value out of very large datasets.
Familiarity with machine learning concepts is an asset.
Strong analytical skills with the ability to problem solve well-judged decisions.
Strategic mindset, with a keen sense of priorities, along with an ability to pivot as the landscape changes.
Strong team-player with the ability to engage with all levels of the organization.
Technical competence using software programs, including but not limited to, Google Suite for business (Sheets, Docs, Slides).
Strong communications and creativity skills with the ability to link data insights to marketing initiatives and use data to tell a story.
Knowledge and experience with smart cities, transportation analytics.
Proven experience in data cleaning, with the ability to identify, analyze, and interpret inconsistencies or inaccuracies in data.
Strong critical thinking abilities, with experience leveraging data to make well-informed recommendations and decisions.

About the job
Connor, Clark & Lunn Financial Group (CCLFG)

Vancouver, BC

We are looking for a Data Analyst to join our Vancouver based Data Management Team.

The Data Management Team (DMT) resides within the middle office and is responsible for managing data centric processes and data quality that supports the investment management business. Connor, Clark & Lunn Financial Group Ltd. (CCLFG) manages a wide range of global assets and heavily relies on the output of the DMT for a variety of functions from the front office to the back. This is a fantastic opportunity to be part of a dynamic strategic team whose scope and importance continues to grow enterprise wide.

We place a high value on maintaining an entrepreneurial spirit and creating a culture where each of us have opportunities to succeed. We are a solution orientated and collaborative team seeking likeminded individuals who thrive in a challenging and dynamic environment. This is a Vancouver based role, which offers a flexibility between working from home and the office.

What You Will Do

This role operates in a unique position, working closely with front office traders, investment managers and a wide range of investment-operation business unit in the middle and back-office. 
You will use your financial and technical knowledge, to provide critical investment data inputs to the whole investment operations process. Our analysts are empowered to thrive as process owners, with both the creativity and responsibility that comes with delegation. Our team continuously strives to identify improvements to operations to scale and grow with the business; you will work highly collaboratively with your team members and dedicated development teams to execute.

Key Responsibilities Include

Security Master: Maintain and validate accuracy of equity/fixed income/derivative data across multiple systems/databases to enable Investment Manager modeling, trading, and risk monitoring.
Process Manager: Manage and enable a myriad of scheduled processes for vendor systems, internal and market data transfers, valuation, and benchmarking data inputs to the investment process.
Data Quality: Deliver timely data signoffs to investment teams; develop and analyze data-quality exceptions and ensure timely resolution.
Stakeholder Service: Provide analysis on operational needs, ad-hoc data/data-history requests for multiple business partners to support pre- and post-trade portfolio management functions.
Process Improvement: Identify process/workflow improvements to increase operational efficiency, mitigate risk, improve data-quality, and increase service levels provided to stakeholders.
Support other operational or engineering staff, senior or managers on a variety of ad-hoc tasks and projects.

What You Bring

Industry Knowledge – Some experience in the investment management industry with exposure to equity, fixed income, and/or derivatives would be ideal. 1-2 years would be an asset.
Education – You have a degree in Finance, Commerce, Business Administration, Business Operations, or a related field. Relevant designation, such as the MBA, CFA, or FRM is an asset.
Problem Solver / Technical – You possess an analytical mindset and able to break down complex processes into components to logically deduce the root cause of issues in data and technology.
Collaborative – You have a collaborative spirit that helps you to work well with others and you communicate effectively to team/cross-team members, and upward to key stakeholders.
Self-Motivated – You have a passion for advancing the quality, scale, and efficiency of data processes and can take ownership of multiple processes with keen attention to detail.
Continuous Process Improvement Mindset – You constantly take a critical eye to processes with the goal of finding improvement opportunities and bring an ability to manage multiple projects.

The salary range for this position is $60,000 - $90,000. The salary range provided reflects the base salary range for this position as required by legislation. In addition, there is an annual performance bonus which contributes to the total compensation of this position. Further questions may be directed to the HR team during the interview process.

About Connor, Clark & Lunn Financial Group

CCLFG provides a broad range of traditional and alternative investment products and services to individuals, advisors, and institutional investors. Our business comprises of eleven institutional investment affiliates that are responsible for investment decision making and client service, as well as distribution. CCLFG partners with each of its affiliates by contributing world class operations, product development expertise, broad distribution, and business management. We have grown from $29 billion in assets and 200 people in 2008 to over $110 billion in assets and over 800 employees today. This has been accompanied by a high level of change in technology, types of assets managed, trading activity and geographic growth. As we look forward, we can see both opportunities and challenges for further growth that only reinforce our commitment to attracting, retaining, and motivating the most talented people.

About the job
Revenu Québec souhaite recruter une ou un analyste en intelligence d’affaires et analytique RH qui occupera un emploi régulier. Nous recrutons au(x) endroit(s) suivant(s) : toutes les régions du Québec. Le lieu de travail sera déterminé en fonction de la personne sélectionnée.

De nouveaux défis, c’est juste ici!

Travailler chez nous, c’est se réaliser grâce à l’énergie collective. C’est aussi contribuer à bâtir une société plus équitable.

Faites partie de notre équipe et occupez un emploi gratifiant tout en bénéficiant de nombreux avantages, dont les suivants :

Votre contribution à la mission de Revenu Québec

Le Service de l’information en ressources humaines de Revenu Québec, c’est une équipe dynamique de six personnes responsables de programmer des étapes de gestion des données (tri, sélection, agrégation, création de variables et croisements) afin d’exploiter, de forer, de valider et d’analyser différents indicateurs relatifs aux activités de gestion des ressources humaines (RH). Ces travaux permettent à l’équipe de concevoir des outils innovants, de produire des tableaux de bord et des états de situation ainsi que de formuler des recommandations qui faciliteront la prise de décisions, la planification d’activités et l’élaboration de programmes en RH, entre autres.

L’équipe s’appuie sur sa combinaison d’expertises techniques et sur sa compréhension des différents contextes d’affaires en RH pour guider d’autres équipes ayant diverses expertises et compétences en RH ainsi que pour collaborer avec celles-ci.

En évoluant au sein de cette équipe, vous collaborerez avec vos collègues en vue de relever des défis stimulants qui visent à faire évoluer l’offre de service en analytique RH. La capacité d’extraire et d’analyser des données en RH, la compréhension des indicateurs et la capacité de mettre ces éléments en relation pour guider l’organisation dans ses décisions en RH sont quelques-unes des compétences que vous mettrez à profit dans votre travail au quotidien.

Votre quotidien à Revenu Québec

En tant qu’analyste en intelligence d’affaires et analytique RH, vous devrez

identifier, documenter ainsi que programmer des requêtes et des méthodologies de calcul afin de répondre aux besoins des demandeuses ou demandeurs d’informations de gestion en RH;
extraire et manipuler des données afin de produire et d’analyser les informations de gestion en RH requises pour le suivi des activités et la reddition de comptes organisationnelle en RH; 
mettre en place des indicateurs et des tableaux de bord pour dégager des tendances, identifier des enjeux, cerner des préoccupations et mesurer les progrès réalisés;
répondre à des demandes ponctuelles d’information et rendre accessibles des informations pertinentes à différents intervenants, dans le respect du caractère confidentiel des dossiers; 
réaliser divers travaux de recherche et formuler des recommandations destinés à la haute direction pour soutenir la prise de décisions;
contribuer à l’identification, à l’analyse et à l’évaluation des besoins d’affaires en analytique RH, tout en étant à l’affût des tendances du marché et des enjeux auxquels l’organisation est confrontée.

En prime, vous aurez l’occasion de vous épanouir professionnellement grâce au soutien d’une équipe expérimentée qui aura à cœur votre réussite et votre avancement.

Les prérequis

Pour vous joindre à notre équipe, vous devez 

détenir un diplôme d’études universitaires équivalant à une 16e année d’études dans l’un des domaines suivants ou dans tout autre domaine jugé pertinent :
informatique de la science des données et de l’intelligence d’affaires,
administration des affaires,
économie, mathématiques ou statistiques,
informatique de gestion;
détenir les connaissances nécessaires pour programmer en utilisant un langage de programmation tel que SAS, SQL ou Python, ou tout autre outil d’analyse des données;
avoir le statut de citoyen canadien ou celui de résident permanent, ou encore être titulaire d’un permis de travail valide au Canada. 

Les éléments suivants pourraient être considérés comme des atouts :

avoir travaillé dans le domaine des ressources humaines;
détenir un certificat universitaire de 1er cycle en analyse des systèmes d’affaires.

Quelques précisions

Vos qualités professionnelles

Ce poste vous plaira si vous 

avez des habiletés relationnelles marquées;
démontrez une bonne capacité d’analyse et de synthèse;
êtes autonome et savez travailler en équipe, avec un minimum de supervision;
faites preuve de curiosité et d’initiative; 
avez une grande capacité d’adaptation aux nouveaux environnements technologiques;
êtes une personne minutieuse, rigoureuse et ayant un bon sens de l’organisation et des priorités.

More About The Role

As a Senior Business Data Analyst, using your analytical and programming background together with your problem-solving skills, you will help extract the secrets of our data, translating data findings into customer insights. You will do so by discovering and transforming the data, performing ad-hoc data analysis, and developing data tools and dashboards for the Marketing Retention team to allow them to monitor the essential metrics to identify pain points and improve business outcomes. You are curious about data, passionate about telling stories based on data, and willing to be data experts of reference within the organization.

Implement data hygiene, data standardization, and data transformation that optimizes other data processes. 
Partner with different team members to solve data problems, identify trends, and find opportunities. 

About You

You have 5+ years of progressive experience in a data analyst role including data mining, data transformation, and delivering relevant insights.
You have 3+ years of experience in programming with SQL, Python, or R for exploring and transforming data within a relational database environment.

You have 2+ years of experience in Statistical Testing (Frequentist A/B testing, Bayesian A/B testing, or Multivariate testing) and design of experiments.
Passion for working in a marketing team of a B2C product and for applying data analytics to improve business results.

Role Summary

As a Data Analyst for Payroll Implementation, your primary responsibility will be to analyze and interpret data related to the implementation of a new payroll system. You will work closely with the project team to gather and validate data, perform data cleansing and transformation, and provide insights and recommendations based on your analysis.

Key Responsibilities

 Collaborate with the project team to understand data requirements for the payroll system implementation.
 Gather, validate, and analyze data from various sources, ensuring data accuracy and completeness.
 Perform data cleansing and transformation to ensure data consistency and integrity.
 Develop and maintain data models, reports, and dashboards to visualize and present data analysis findings.
 Identify trends, patterns, and anomalies in data, and provide insights and recommendations to optimize payroll processes.
 Work closely with stakeholders to understand their data analysis needs and provide customized reports and analysis.
 Collaborate with IT teams to ensure data integration and migration from legacy systems to the new payroll system.
 Perform data validation and reconciliation to ensure data accuracy and consistency between different systems.
 Assist in the development and implementation of data quality control measures to ensure data integrity.
 Stay updated with industry best practices and trends in data analysis and implement them in the payroll implementation process.



Key Qualifications/Requirements

 Bachelor's degree in Data Science, Statistics, Computer Science, or a related field.
 Proven experience as a data analyst or similar role, preferably in the payroll domain.
 Strong proficiency in data analysis and visualization tools such as SQL, Excel, Power BI, or Tableau.
 Excellent data manipulation and data cleansing skills.
 Knowledge of database management systems, data warehousing, and data integration concepts.
 Strong analytical and problem-solving skills.
 Ability to interpret complex data and present insights in a clear and concise manner.
 Strong attention to detail and accuracy in data analysis.
 Ability to work effectively in a team and collaborate with cross-functional stakeholders.
 Knowledge of payroll processes, systems, and compliance requirements is an asset.

Field Competitive Intelligence Analyst, Americas (Remote CT/MT) 

About The Role

As a Field Competitive Intelligence Analyst, you will support the CrowdStrike Sales and Executive Teams. You will work and support the CTO Labs and Field CTO Teams team at CrowdStrike. The Field CI team’s mission is to identify & deliver key competitive differentiators to support the international growth of customers, new markets, and TAM. This includes driving strategy through cross functional collaboration across the company including Product, Sales, Marketing, and more.

As the Field CI Analyst, you will be responsible for creating and communicating the company’s competitive differentiation strategy on a regional basis and working closely with the company’s product CTO’s, Product Managers and Field functions on a regular basis. You will also work closely with other groups within CrowdStrike, which includes: marketing, value management, legal and corporate affairs teams.

This role reports to the Manager, Competitive Intelligence Strategy. With your extensive cybersecurity background and your ability to think and operate at a strategic level, you will drive CrowdStrike’s technical vision and strategy and support on strategic engagements across the CrowdStrike organization.

What You'll Do

Support current customers and new customers by sharing CrowdStrike’s key competitive value differentiators, supporting the positioning of CrowdStrike as the leading thought leader for Cybersecurity with customers, partners, and analysts.
Driving and communicating CrowdStrike’s technology strategy to customers and partners as well as industry events.
Maintaining an in-depth knowledge of the cyber security industry, the competitive landscape and related industry developments to ensure we continue to be thought leaders who innovate ahead of the market.
Using stakeholders’ feedback to inform necessary improvements and adjustments to technology.
Focusing on technology improvements that will improve competitive positioning of the CrowdStrike products.
Providing recommendations for continuous improvement.

What You'll Need

Deep technical and operations skills in understanding the capabilities (strengths and weaknesses) of competitor offerings.
Strong analytical and communication skills to allow translation of competitive differentiation points into contextually relevant talking points.
Demonstrate a deep and broad knowledge of security issues and trends and are able to articulate a high-level security strategy to both technical and non-technical audiences.
Working in a role such as or similar to Competitive Strategist, Strategic Consultant, Enterprise Security Architect.
Experience with/exposure to Endpoint Security, Cloud Security, SIEM/Log Management, Mobile Security, Identity Security, Incident Response as well as other cyber security domains.
Regional travel is expected on a limited basis.

About the job
What you'll do 

* Reporting to the Reporting and Analytics Team Lead, this role will be part of a team that is responsible for providing Human Resources reporting and analytics that leverage the information in our SAP Human Capital Management (HCM) system. 

* This role is responsible for producing regular reporting deliverables, including HR metrics and dashboards; responding to ad hoc reporting and analytics inquiries; and contributing to enterprise reporting initiatives (e.g. enterprise dashboards, annual report, and Regulatory reporting). 

* This role is also responsible for maintaining and continuously improving reports in the HCM system and the end-to-end implementation of any report enhancements. 

* In addition, the position will help coordinate and further develop tools and processes to continuously improve and expand the reporting and analytics shared services model. 

* As a member of the overall HR Systems and Analytics Tier 2 SAP support team, this role will work collaboratively with other team members to support the end users of the HR SAP HCM system, also working work closely with both our Tier 1 (Employee Service Centre) and Tier 3 (SAP Technology) support teams. 

* In this role, the successful candidate will also have opportunities to collaborate with other Human Resources departments and other functional areas within the organization. 

What you bring 

* Must have an undergraduate degree, diploma, or certificate in Human Resources or a related discipline, or equivalent combination of education and experience. 

* Must have experience doing reporting and analytical work using Microsoft Excel, including analysis of data using advanced Excel formulas, functions, and pivot tables. 

* Must have a minimum 1-2 years of experience working with a Human Resources Information System (HRIS); SAP HCM experience in particular is an asset. 

* Must have a minimum 1-2 years of relevant Human Resources experience. 

* Strong client service orientation, and able to build/maintain strong working relationships. 

* Experience with cloud based HCM solutions would be an asset. 

* Excellent communication skills (both verbal and written), strong interpersonal, presentation, and organizational skills, and attention to detail. 

* Strong research, analytical, and problem solving skills are required. 

* SharePoint Administration experience would be an asset. 

* Experience with Data Visualization software, particularly Tableau, PowerBI, SAP Analytics Cloud would be an asset. 

* CPHR designation would be an asset.

The candidate should have a general understanding of Geoscience and Environmental Data Management. Position Description

We are currently seeking driven and intellectually curious individuals who want to be part of a growing and passionate team that is developing industry leading approaches to discretionary investment research.

We are recruiting for a Senior Associate/Portfolio Manager Sector Data Analyst to integrate data driven insights into the alpha generation process by leveraging alternative data in supporting sector focused investment teams. The goal is to help make better data driven investment decisions.

Directly support fundamental sector focused investment teams by leveraging the relevant data to answer investment questions
Act as sector data domain expert by becoming deeply familiar with industry datasets including sourcing and evaluating data, building data products and conducting bespoke research

Proactively seek ways to advance investment research by sourcing new data and analytics

About the job
We’re building a relationship-oriented bank for the modern world. We need talented, passionate professionals who are dedicated to doing what’s right for our clients.

What You’ll Be Doing

The goal of CIBC’s Capital Markets business is to be the premier client-focused Capital Markets based in Canada. To deliver on this, the capital markets arm of CIBC provides a wide range of credit, capital markets, investment banking, merchant banking and research products and services to government, institutional, corporate and retail clients in Canada and in key markets around the world

Reporting to the Director, Projects and Initiatives, the Business Analyst (BA) will support the project team in conducting and managing the data analysis, migration planning, and related activities, including the creation of a detailed migration plan based on results drawn from the data analysis. In addition, the BA will assist in preparing reports, dashboards, timelines, and source feeds with relevant and accurate data from the Capital Markets client onboarding and regulatory application (CORA) database to upstream/downstream systems.

The objective of the work is to support the migration of data, client profiles/cases, audit history, and documents from the current global and regional KYC/AML CORA platform to a new platform and ensure that Capital Markets meet the client data requirements specific for its line of business according to the Enterprise Data Governance policies and standards. All activities and reports/dashboards are to be provided in a high-quality and timely manner as per the project timeline.

At CIBC, we enable the work environment most optimal for you to thrive in your role. You’ll have the flexibility to manage your work activities within a hybrid work arrangement where you’ll spend 3 days per week on-site, while other days will be remote.

How You’ll Succeed

Data Analysis and Migration planning - Conduct detailed analysis of our current data sets from the CORA database to assess what data, cases, history, and documents, etc. should be prepared for migration, what data remediation is needed, and what is the impact on upstream/downstream systems. Develop data mapping from legacy system to the target data structure in the new environment, ensuring data compatibility and consistency. Lead the discussions to determine future data needs and design and document the processes that will support such needs. Preparation of project artifacts such as data flow diagrams, impact analysis, status reports, and ensure that the data analysis work package meet the project’s objectives within the defined timelines.
Client Life Cycle Framework and CORA - Be very familiar with the data collection and capture process in the Capital Markets Client Onboarding space and the overall mandate of the Client Onboarding and AML Risk Review teams (Regional Onboarding, Offboarding, Regular Review, etc.). Work with the regional client onboarding and risk review teams within Client Services, who are the primary users of CORA, and with our partners in Technology and the Client Data Management teams to identify areas where quality of client data can be improved, which may require manual cleanup and remediation efforts.
Technology Savvy – Working with our Technology partners, able to apply technical and business knowledge to the formulation of practical business solutions for Client Services. Must be familiar at a high-level with cloud-based data migration solutions, server and database infrastructures, and have experience with data migration across different platforms and systems. Proficiency in data extraction and transformation tools, strong SQL querying and scripting skills, knowledge of ETL (Extract, Transform, Load) processes and ETL software, and familiarity with data modeling and database design principles. Proficiency in data cleansing and data validation techniques, knowledge of data integration and consolidation methods, expertise in data profiling and data quality assessment, and understanding of data warehousing concepts and practices.
Attention to Detail and Independence - Work within a challenging, fast-paced environment where priorities often shift and time pressures demand a rapid response to requests. Focused attention to detail when conducting all assigned activities, which may include but are not limited to analysis, process and reporting design, writing procedures as well as other project tasks as needed. Must be able to seize concepts, understand current processes quickly, and learn independently. While not hesitating to ask questions when necessary; and always keeping the manager well-informed of progress.
Good understanding of Change Management – Understand the importance of the role of project sponsor, project manager, Client Services and other stakeholders who are the principal system users while creating the migration plan. Able to articulate the various aspects of change management including awareness, desire, knowledge, ability and reinforcement for the migration plan. Preparing for change management success includes writing communication and training plans. 
Collaboration and Communication – Work closely with the vendor and collaborate with data engineers/developers to profile source data. Provide timely updates to stakeholders, including the Project Manager and Client Services head. Urgently escalate any challenges or roadblocks to the data migration project, and collaborate with relevant teams to find timely solutions.

Who You Are

You have relevant experience. You have 3-5 years of working experience in the financial, technology, or relevant industry along with a good understanding of KYC/AML Regulatory requirements and processing infrastructures. Experience working with Client Lifecycle Management vendors such as Fenergo, and previous experience leading System Data Migration projects will be a strong asset.
You have Business knowledge. Understanding of Capital Markets infrastructure, systems/applications, and businesses/products. As well as, Client Onboarding procedures. 
You give meaning to Data. Excellent analytical and reporting skills using Microsoft Excel and other business intelligence, analytics and data visualization tools, e.g., Tableau, Alteryx, and Power BI, to produce relevant analysis, reports, and display data to meet the needs of the project and Stakeholders.
You demonstrate experience in enhancements on automation, report simplification and streamlining forecasting/planning processes
You are Detail Oriented. Must be vigilant in delivering results, have strong attention to detail, good planning skills and the ability to overcome obstacles. Maintain a sense of urgency and ability to prioritize multiple deliverables
You act like an owner. A "can do" attitude is a must, with a passion for driving analysis and solutions. Ability to successfully influence different groups and individuals to deliver high-quality and timely deliverables. Ability to directly address conflicts and escalate issues, where appropriate. Highly organized and strong results orientation that includes adherence to deadlines while maintaining high-quality results/output. Strong sense of accountability and ownership over all assignments and activities
You are a strong communicator. Ability to present to an audience and communicate effectively at all levels of the organization, including clients and front-office individuals
You have strong writing skills. Ability to write well-structured and well-formatted procedures and job aids in English using clear, plain and simple language for easy reference and understanding by the reader. All documents should have names of the writer(s) and reviewer(s) and signoff date(s)
You have good project management skills. Ability to successfully navigate a complex organizational structure that involves numerous groups and individuals. Excellent problem-solving and time-management skills. Adaptable, flexible and willing to work in a dynamic environment. Comfortable working with a team and individually to deliver results
Values matter to you. You bring your real self to work and live our values - trust, teamwork, and accountability.

Assurer le leadership dans l'élaboration des nouveaux outils jusqu’à leur mise en service. 
Collaborer activement aux activités et initiatives d'amélioration continue de l’équipe.

Primary Responsibilities
Promote a data-driven culture to identify areas of opportunity and support eCommerce and digital product teams in improving the digital experience.

Lead analysis by interpreting complex data, modeling using statistical techniques, validating results, and communicating to senior management.
Prepare reports, create presentations and present actionable recommendations to support eCommerce and Marketing initiatives.
Partner with digital product teams to identify issues and opportunities to eliminate points of friction and improve conversion rate.
Build and maintain reports to monitor digital effectiveness and provide actionable insights on digital performance to optimize engagement and improve core KPIs.
Leverage multiple data sources to profile and segment digital customers and understand the customer journey, assisting in the development of long-term strategic objectives for digital adoption.
Work with technology partners to establish and implement Google Analytics site tagging practices and tracking requirements.
Establish A/B testing framework and roadmap to conduct testing, analyze results and provide recommendations to inform project prioritization.
Provide in-depth reporting to enable discussions regarding results, trends and insights with regional leaders and identify opportunities to drive adoption and penetration.
Monitor online customer churn and proactively provide reporting to eBusiness field support and Regional Leaders to re-engage with at-risk accounts.
Provide data and ad hoc reports as needed to support business case development and/or inclusion in communications to leadership across the organization.
Support eBusiness and Marketing in establishing KPI reporting framework to measure effectiveness of online promotions and campaigns.
Leverage analytics and a “test & iterate” approach to help guide program/campaign development.
Develop post implementation reviews on campaigns and programs driving digital adoption.
Partner with BI to ensure accuracy, consistency, relevance and timeliness of data provided to the business

About the job
Why join us?

Are you looking to join a dynamic pension plan that embodies the strong values of its 500,000 members and is an industry leading global investor? If so, we would love to tell you our story.

At OMERS we put our people first and are proud to embrace the diversity of thought and leadership that comes from having locations in Toronto, London, New York, Singapore, Sydney and other major cities across North America and Europe. Quantitative Analyst, Portfolio Analytics

OMERS Total Portfolio Management manages the public markets investment portfolio consisting of fixed income (including government bonds, Inflation-Linked Bonds and public and private credit) and equities, including global public equities, intellectual property and structured investments. The team’s approach is focused on generating current income from high-quality assets and generating a consistent capital return with a lower volatility than the broad markets. We also seek to develop strategic partnerships with best-in-class investors to access credit and other opportunities on a global basis. The OMERS Capital Markets' team is distinguished by its diversity in expertise and experience and its commitment to reliable, lower-risk performance. Our objective is to construct a well-diversified portfolio that will deliver long-term annualized returns in the 6 to 9% range.

Job Description

As a member of the OMERS Total Portfolio Management (TPM) team in Toronto, reporting to the Director, Head of Portfolio Analytics, you will contribute and lead our transformation of how Capital Markets improves investment decision making through data driven insights.

As a Quantitative Analyst, Portfolio Analytics, at OMERS Total Portfolio Management, you will be part of a team that are building world-class analytics and quantitative tools. The role provides the successful candidate with the opportunity to work closely with the Global Credit team, where you will develop and grow your understanding of quantitative and technical tools that drive the development of the systematic components of portfolio management.

As a member of the Total Portfolio Management team, you will be responsible for the following 

Developing analytics, tools and processes required to manage diverse flavours of data
Applying quantitative skills to systematically ensure high data quality
Developing, structuring and querying SQL databases
Developing and maintaining daily, systematic processes required for Global Credit’s portfolio
Building credit instrument pricing engines to facilitate daily portfolio management, back-testing and stress-testing
Working closely with IT to establish new ETLs and optimize existing ETLs
Effectively communicate highly technical subject matter to Global Credit Portfolio Managers
Communicating and working regularly with traders, portfolio managers, internal and external managers, and operations staff to gain a holistic view on quantitative portfolio management as it relates to Global Credit

You Bring The Following Skills And Qualifications

Bachelor’s degree in Computer Science, Mathematics, Business, or related field.
3+ years of relevant experience
Familiarity with Python and SQL is required
Experience working within a credit investment team is an asset
Experience with data engineering and/or data quality assurance is an asset
Experience with data visualization such as Plotly is an asset
Experience with Power BI (or equivalence dashboarding tool) is preferred
Experience with financial tools or software e.g. Bloomberg, CRD.
A passion around learning new technologies and analytical techniques
Strong attention to detail, highly organized and keen to learn
Ability to work independently and within a team
An action-oriented approach with a high degree of initiative and ability to deliver results
Strong written and verbal communication skills
Highly developed interpersonal and relationship management skills

Challenges and Opportunities 

The role involves using highly sensitive information for making business decisions.
Candidates must be able to prioritize multiple tasks to complete deliverables in a timely fashion.
The role could require occasional conversation with our Asia trading team as we develop more analytics.

OMERS is offering 

An Inclusive work environment which celebrates diversity

Collaborative, innovative, and focused approach with high quality investments

Our story

Founded in 1962, OMERS is one of Canada’s largest defined benefit pension plans, with $127.4 billion in net assets as at June 30, 2023. OMERS is a jointly-sponsored pension plan, with more than 1,000 participating employers ranging from large cities to local agencies, and over half a million active, deferred and retired members. OMERS members include union and non-union employees of municipalities, school boards, local boards, transit systems, electrical utilities, emergency services and children’s aid societies across Ontario. Contributions to the Plan are funded equally by members and employers. OMERS teams work in Toronto, London, New York, Amsterdam, Luxembourg, Singapore, Sydney and other major cities across North America and Europe – serving members and employers and originating and managing a diversified portfolio of high-quality investments in public markets, private equity, infrastructure and real estate.

OMERS is committed to having a workforce that reflects the communities in which we live and work. We are an equal opportunity employer committed to a barrier-free recruitment and selection process. At OMERS inclusion and diversity means belonging. How we create a sense of belonging is through our employees and our vast network of Employee Resource Groups. Whether you are passionate about gender, pride, or visible minorities, we have groups that are focused on making a difference in all of our lives.

YOUR MISSION

We are looking for a qualified and motivated Data Business Analyst to join our Customer Data & Analytics team, which is divided into three sub-teams: data analysts, data engineers, and a dedicated team for the Customer Data Platform (CDP) project.

As a Data Business Analyst, you will play a crucial role in bridging the gap between data-driven insights and business strategy. You will be responsible for aligning data expert teams and establishing best practices in report management and data usage.

Main Responsibilities

 Collaborate with cross-functional teams to understand their data needs and translate those requirements into actionable reports and recommendations.
 Present findings and insights to stakeholders, assisting them in making data-informed decisions.
 Work closely with business units to identify data requirements and create data specifications for projects.
 Define key performance indicators (KPIs) and metrics to measure business performance.
 Assist in establishing data governance and data management best practices within the organization.
 Ensure compliance with data protection and privacy regulations (e.g., GDPR, CCPA).
 Utilize data analytics and visualization tools (e.g., SQL, Python, Tableau, Power BI) to manipulate and present data effectively.
 Working closely with external agencies that support some analytical and data science activities.
 Stay current with industry trends and best practices in data analysis and business intelligence.

YOUR UNIQUE EXPERTISE

 Bachelor's degree in a related field (e.g., Business, Information Systems, Statistics).
 Proven experience in data analysis and business intelligence.
 Proficiency in data analysis tools and programming languages (SQL, Python, etc.).
 Familiarity with data visualization tools (Tableau, Power BI, etc.).
 Knowledge of the Cloud (Google Cloud Platform).
 Strong problem-solving skills and attention to detail.
 Excellent communication and interpersonal skills to collaborate with various stakeholders.
 Strong business acumen and the ability to link data insights to business outcomes.
 Knowledge of data governance and privacy regulations is a plus.
 Knowledge of a Customer Data Platform (CDP) is a plus.
 Bilingualism (French/English) is preferred.

Why Mozilla?

Mozilla Corporation is the non-profit-backed technology company that has shaped the internet for the better over the last 25 years. We make pioneering brands like Firefox, the privacy-minded web browser, and Pocket, a service for keeping up with the best content online. Now, with more than 225 million people around the world using our products each month, we’re shaping the next 25 years of technology and helping to reclaim an internet built for people, not companies. Our work focuses on diverse areas including AI, social media, security and more. And we’re doing this while never losing our focus on our core mission – to make the internet better for people.

The Mozilla Corporation is wholly owned by the non-profit 501(c) Mozilla Foundation. This means we aren’t beholden to any shareholders — only to our mission. Along with 60,000+ volunteer contributors and collaborators all over the world, Mozillians design, build and distribute open-source software that enables people to enjoy the internet on their terms.

TD Description

Our Values
At TD we're guided by our purpose is to enrich the lives of our customers, communities and colleagues, and share a set of values that shape our culture and guide our behavior. In exchange for how our colleagues show up to help TD succeed, we are committed to delivering a colleague experience grounded in Impact, Growth and a Culture of Care. No matter where you work across TD, we empower you to make an impact at work and in your community, explore and grow your career and be part of our caring and inclusive culture.

Making Your Well-being a Priority
A supportive culture that promotes colleague well-being is core to who we are. At TD, we focus on total well-being with extensive programs to help colleagues assess, manage, and improve their well-being across four core pillars — physical, financial, social and mental/emotional. In addition, we champion a safe and inclusive work environment so colleagues feel a sense of belonging and feel supported in their personal and professional growth. Through our focus on well-being, we know that we can help our colleagues thrive, contribute to our culture of care, and support better business outcomes, because when colleagues feel their best, they're more likely to do their best.

Our Total Rewards Package
Our Total Rewards package reflects the investment we make in our colleagues to help them, and their families achieve their well-being goals. Total Rewards at TD includes a base salary, variable compensation, and several other key plans such as health and well-being benefits including medical, dental, vision & mental health coverage, savings and retirement programs, paid time off, banking benefits and discounts, career development, and reward and recognition programs.

How We Work
At TD, we believe in-person connections fuel collaboration and collective creativity. Our workplace experience empowers colleagues to do great work side-by-side at TD locations, while offering flexibility to work remotely where it makes sense for the work and team. Our teams work in one of three workplace models: Hybrid, Onsite and Primarily Remote. Wherever our colleagues are working, they’ll always have access to the TD community and experience our culture of care.

Who We Are
TD is one of the world's leading global financial institutions and is the fifth largest bank in North America by branches. Every day, we deliver legendary customer experiences to over 27 million households and businesses in Canada, the United States and around the world. More than 95,000 TD colleagues bring their skills, talent, and creativity to the Bank, those we serve, and the economies we support.
