Job Description

About this Role

This role is responsible for monitoring fraud trends, investigating emerging threats and quickly developing and deploying new strategies to manage those threats. 
The strategist 
Must balance loss decisions with the impact to operational teams and the customer experience. 
Is expected to develop and apply deep fraud and process expertise, and to leverage sophisticated tools/detection systems to manage risk/reward balance. 

The successful candidate will work collaboratively with a diverse team of operational agents, Fraud solution developers, data scientists, business insights analysts and subject matter experts and applies fraud business expertise leveraging advanced tools and detection systems to manage risk appropriately. The incumbent will be accountable for loss and customer experience targets.


Accountabilities:

Fraud Loss Management
Reviews daily fraud attacks to create segmentation and develop/implement fraud strategies while balancing the impact to the operational teams and customer experience
Design and develop advanced analytics tools to derive business insights from data and information
Makes adjustments to shifting network rules, liability requirements or other exogenous factors
Executes strategy design and configuration in all fraud prevention platforms (e.g. Faclon, TSYS, FIS, SQN, PRM, Citadel, DPS, VCas, Avant, Experian, Transunion), in alignment with the Change Management protocols
Supports case valuation and prioritization to optimize fraud management
Become a subject matter expert on the end-to-end operational process, transaction liability and regulatory requirements

Process Support
Produce timely diagnostics to identify system, strategy and operational issues
Participates in defect analysis to identify and remediate fraud coverage gaps
Identify and assess new developing fraud trends as they evolve
Participates in the creation of monitoring and reporting by defining requirements and performing validation

Partner Support
Maintain strong relationships with internal stakeholders such as Fraud Operations
Support the continuous improvement agenda for our operational partners

 

Job Requirements
What can you bring to TD? 

Undergraduate degree from a technical domain (e.g. mathematics/statistics, computer science, engineering) 5 Years +
Experience working with big data management and analytics tools
Proficiency in a data extraction/analysis/visualization tool. Examples include: SQL, Python, SAS, Knowledge Seeker, Excel, Tableau
Demonstrated analytical, modeling and problem solving skills 
Creative, Critical, Conceptual thinker, ability to wade through data and arrive at conclusions
Ability to communicate strategy analysis to both technical and non-technical team members, either verbally or via documentation 
Ability to take initiative and work independently under tight timelines
Ability to work collaboratively and build relationships
Motivated to constantly strive to find innovative ways to enhance capabilities

Preferable
Experience in fraud management is an asset
Knowledge of machine learning is an asset

Our story

Oxford Properties Group (“Oxford”) is a leading global real estate investor, asset manager and business builder. It builds, buys, and grows defined real estate operating business with world-class management teams. Established in 1960, Oxford and its portfolio companies manage approximately C$87 billion of assets across four continents on behalf of their investment partners. Oxford’s owned portfolio encompasses office, logistics, retail, multifamily residential, life sciences, hotels, alternatives and credit in global gateway cities and high-growth hubs. A thematic investor with a committed source of capital, Oxford invests in properties, portfolios, development sites, debt, securities, and real estate businesses across the risk-reward spectrum. Together with its portfolio companies, Oxford is one of the world’s most active developers with over 80 projects currently underway globally across all major asset classes. Oxford is owned by OMERS, the Canadian defined benefit pension plan for Ontario's municipal employees.

For more information on Oxford, visit www.oxfordproperties.com

Purpose

The Senior BI Analyst & UX Designer, Sales Reporting & Analytics is responsible for oversight, maintenance and governance of the different systems used to analyze vast amounts of data from different sources, and deploy interactive, infographic visualizations & dashboards to sales and senior management. They will provide subject matter expertise to management on opportunities and options for technical solutions to business problems, as well as train and develop the Sales Reporting & Analytics team to administer system settings, develop front-end user interfaces, and design eye-popping infographic data visualizations. They will assist the Senior Manager in overseeing data governance of sales reporting. Is this role right for you? In this role you will:

Digital Strategy

Act as subject matter expert with Excel, Access, MicroStrategy, SQL, Salesforce, Broadridge, Power BI, Tableau, and Oracle on Demand
Work with the Senior Manager and Strategic Alliances team to formulate ideas and plans for the creation and use of technology to facilitate business objectives of increasing sales quality of output and operational efficiency
Stay informed of technological trends and their potential application to the business
Stay informed of best practices in innovation and data visualization tools, with a focus on generating actionable insights within captivating dashboards and reporting

Analytics & Reporting

Use varying data mining techniques to design and implement analytics and reporting to support various internal partners and products
Perform analyses to find patterns and extract useful insights, predictions or knowledge from large or varying datasets

Business Process and Continuous Improvement

Data Governance

Develop a structure and process to oversee data integrity in order to properly mine and roll up underlying data for management and sales reporting
Create and maintain a data dictionary to ensure new data is properly maintained, categorized and linked within existing reporting structures
Document all existing reports, their purposes, and end users to determine which reports are redundant, out of date, or no longer being used, to decommission them as required
Create a reporting map to identify how existing reports are affected by new products or business lines, and ensure new data is suppressed from reporting as required

University Degree or equivalent College Diploma

Il n’existe pas d’actif informationnel plus important que les données pour la conduite des affaires de la SAQ. C’est pourquoi nous lançons plusieurs initiatives d'envergure au niveau de la donnée sur les prochaines années, tant pour la gouvernance, la valorisation et l'exploitation des données d’entreprise.

Ta mission :
En tant qu'Architecte de Données d'Entreprise au sein de notre organisation, tu relèveras du directeur, architecture d’entreprise. Tu joueras un rôle crucial dans la conception, le développement et la mise en œuvre de l'architecture de données qui soutient notre stratégie commerciale et nos initiatives technologiques. Tu seras responsable de créer et de maintenir une infrastructure de données robuste, évolutive et sécurisée, qui permettra la collecte, le stockage, la transformation et la mise à disposition efficace des données à travers l'ensemble de l'entreprise.

Tes responsabilités :

Architecture de solution-donnée :
Concevoir des solutions d'architecture de données en tenant compte de la modélisation, de la gestion, de la sécurité et de la performance des données à l'échelle de l'entreprise ;
Développer des schémas de données, des modèles conceptuels et logiques, ainsi que des flux de données pour répondre aux besoins opérationnels et analytiques ;
Collaborer avec les parties prenantes internes, y compris les équipes métier et techniques, pour comprendre les besoins en matière de données et définir les exigences architecturales correspondantes ;


Stratégie de la donnée :
Participer à des initiatives d'innovation en proposant de nouvelles approches pour l'exploitation et l'analyse des données ;
Sélectionner et évaluer les technologies de base de données, les outils d'intégration et les plate formes d'analyse de données en fonction des exigences du projet ;

Intégration de la donnée :
Superviser la mise en œuvre de pipelines de données ETL/ELT et événementiels pour garantir l'intégrité et la qualité des données tout au long du processus ;
Surveiller les performances du système de gestion des données et proposer des améliorations pour optimiser l'efficacité et la disponibilité des données ;
Collaborer avec les équipes d'ingénierie logicielle pour intégrer l'architecture de données dans les applications et les systèmes existants ;

Gouvernance des données :
Assurer la conformité aux normes de sécurité des données et aux réglementations en vigueur, en mettant en œuvre des stratégies de protection des données et des mesures de confidentialité appropriées.

Job Description

Who We Are

BGIS is a leading provider of customized facility management and real estate services. With our combined team of over 6,500 globally, we relentlessly focus on enabling innovation through the services we deliver, while actively looking for new opportunities that will enable innovation for our clients’ businesses. Globally, we manage over 320 million square feet of client portfolios across 30,000+ locations in North America, Europe, Middle East, Australia and Asia. Further information is available at www.bgis.com

Summary

The Fleet Analyst and Logistics Coordinator (FALC) works as an integral member of the back-office team supporting Regional Operations Managers, BGIS ITS Technicians, and senior executives by analyzing the daily operations and maintenance activities necessary for safe, reliable, and efficient operations. They are responsible for keeping all Fleet data files up to date, supporting the planning, scheduling, and analysis of preventative and corrective maintenance activities.

The FALC is a supporting role who will work with the branch contacts to coordinate necessary fleet changes, repairs, GPS installations, maintenance visits, and any training. The FALC is expected to execute this work according to BGIS standard practices and is responsible to effectively maintain an up- to –date fleet list. The FALC is also responsible for supporting in the financial management of the data of the daily vehicle GPS logs, and fleet costs.

Key Duties & Responsibilities

Team Member Support

Acts as a liaison between the Corporate Fleet team and the individual branch managers to drive efficiencies in fleet activities. 
Tracks and follows up with all vehicle maintenance logs and inspection records to ensure accurate and up to date file systems.
Assists local branch support with transfer of vehicles between locations, scheduling repairs and maintenance. 
Meets with various leadership to review any trends in mismatched timecard to GPS data.
Determines and coordinates the distribution of assets based upon provided criteria. 


Reporting and Analysis

Completes high volume file management; ensuring files are complete, accurate, and continually updated.
Maintains weekly GPS extract to compare against the individual technician’s timesheets.
Manages cost reporting by vehicle to ensure real-time data on maintenance, lease, repair costs for the lifetime of the vehicle.
Supports the Regional Managers in scheduling repairs & replacements to ensure the least amount of down time per technician. 


 Inventory Forecast Support

Works with leadership and Corporate Fleet to forecast the purchase of replacement assets in order to maintain accurate inventory levels by location.


Dashboard Development Support

Collaborates with the Strategic Team to develop dashboards for accurate reporting leading in order to drive cost efficiencies. 
Other duties as assigned.


Knowledge & Skills

Business Diploma or Degree, relevant work experience is an asset. 
Display excellent interpersonal and communication skills, both written and verbal is essential.
Ability to pay strong attention to detail.
Ability to multitask, prioritize, stay organized, and perform in a deadline-oriented environment.
Analyze problems and have problem-solving skills.
Work independently as well as in a team-based environment.
Work in a fast-paced environment.
Display strong knowledge of relevant computer applications.
General knowledge of corporate automobile’s considered an asset. 
Strong organizational, coordination and documentation skills with the ability to multi-task.
Proficient with MS Office, specifically advanced Excel skills.


Licenses and/or Professional Accreditation

Valid driver’s license.

About the job
About Grant Thornton Grant Thornton is one of the world’s leading professional services networks with member firms in over 145 countries, 72,000 people and global revenues of $7.5bn. Member firms offer audit, tax, and advisory services to privately owned companies, publicly listed companies, public sector and not for profit organisations, both domestically and internationally.

Grant Thornton International Ltd (GTIL) is the umbrella legal entity for the Grant Thornton global network of member firms. GTIL sets the strategic direction, convenes member firms, connects global communities, and protects the brand and reputation of the network. GTIL and the member firms will continually improve the sustainability of their operations and strive to make a positive impact on clients, people, markets, and the communities in which we operate, in line with the UN’s Sustainable Development Goals (SDGs).

Role purpose 

In our Go Beyond network strategy 2025 our vision is to become ‘the most valued network in the profession’.

This role sits within the International Business Support Function (IBSF) at GTIL. The Function exists to support member firms win more international business. Talking our clients’ language – and understanding the broader commercial issues and trends affecting their businesses – is critical to winning and expanding international client relationships in all geographies.

One of the ways in which we do this is by equipping our engagement partners with the knowledge, content and contacts they need to have quality conversations with their industry clients.

This new role will work with our Associate Director – Policy and Data, to deliver the global policy and data strategic objectives.

Main Responsibilities 

Policy Management
Manage GTConnect IBSF policy pages
Obtain awareness of market practice and stakeholder expectation and audit and review policies for updating

Contribute to new policy and policy update projects including editing and drafting of policies.
Track usage metrics of policies and report to IBSF Team Leadership

 Data Management Responsibilities
Provide routine global business development reporting and ad hoc data analysis focused on IBSF areas of responsibility
Liaise directly with IBSF leadership to stay informed on new business activity (including pursuit, industry, business development, and targeting)
Maintain internal databases and manage data cleaning and validation processes
Help prepare presentations for internal meetings, business reviews, etc.
Provide data visuals and statistical analysis for corporate reports and presentations
Liaise with Finance to ensure accurate revenue and referral data is captured for firm reporting
Focus on enhancing, streamlining, and automating processes to create efficiencies

 Technology Liaison Responsibilities
Assist Associate Director, Policy and Data in liaising with Information Security and Information Technology teams to upgrade existing firm tech infrastructure to better enable business insights
Execute project management tasks for technology projects including note taking, meeting scheduling, and slide deck creation and management.

 Analysis Responsibilities
Conduct strategic analysis on internal and external data sets (including financial, market, and proprietary data) to develop fact-based insights and recommendations for the International Business Support Function strategy
Assist with business development and strategic projects that support corporate strategy
Conduct exploratory data analysis on existing data sets
Gather and assess new data sets for insights use
Design and conduct data experiments to test and validate hypotheses

IBSF support and wider support
Build awareness of wider IBSF activities and support on ad hoc projects when appropriate
Deploy skills to wider GTIL Policy and Data projects where requested

Benefits 

There are many benefits of being part of Grant Thornton International, working with a global and diverse team in a virtual setting is just one of them. We pride ourselves on our inclusive culture and believe it's one of our most valuable assets. We also recognise the importance of time off at Grant Thornton International. Taking time away can lead to improved wellbeing and better productivity, which is why we don’t cap your leave. So if you need to take that extra Friday off (and Monday too), no problem. We believe work is no longer a location, it is what we do. This should help all of us deliver our best work, while achieving the right balance in our lives. We want to build a culture of virtual inclusivity. One where all our people have the ability to choose what works best for them but also provides our people the best shared working experience utilising the digital tools we have available. GTIL will provide individuals with the necessary support and equipment to work effectively from home. We also have a collaborative space to offer should you prefer working outside of your home. We will offer you access to digital learning options, as well as external training, should you role and development needs require this. We fully understand the importance of balancing your life and we aim to support that with remote working and flexibility within your role. We understand the time you spend outside of work helps shape what you bring into work, so we encourage flexibility on both sides. However, if you prefer to work from the office, this is also something we offer. We also understand the importance of working comfortably in a remote office - most likely your home, which is why we offer all staff a monthly home office allowance to ensure you're well equipped and able to undertake your role to the fullest. Job Overview: As a Senior Analyst (Data Governance Process Analyst) at Electronic Arts, you will help ensure that data is accurate and complete. You will establish Enterprise Data Governance procedures throughout the data lifecycle. You will collaborate with distributed teams to define policies, procedures, strategies and standards to support the Data Governance Framework. Your analytical skills will identify data process and policy needs or issues, and implementing corrective actions. You understand data governance principles, data management best practices, and experience working with large amounts of data used by multiple partners and internal clients.

Responsibilities

Collaborate with partners to understand data requirements.
Develop and implement data governance policy and procedures and conduct compliance.
Create Data Governance process-modelling & documentation.
Develop metrics to monitor data management and infrastructure usage and costs.
Create documentation, procedures & dashboards to improve the Data Governance Framework.
Provide training and support to users of Data Governance products and services.
Ensure compliance with data privacy and regulatory requirements through regular auditing and interviews.
Monitor industry trends and emerging technologies related to data governance.
Work with Product Managers, Data Stewards, Data Architects, Data Analysts & Data Engineers & Infrastructure experts.

Qualifications

At least 5 years Proven experience as a senior analyst, or similar role
Bachelor's degree in Computer Science, Information Systems, Data Analytics, or a related field
Technical skills
Excellent understanding of data governance principles and frameworks and data management practices.
Knowledge of regulatory requirements, reputation protection and compliance standards related to data governance (e.g., GDPR, CCPA).
Proficient in data profiling and analysis using SQL, Python, or other relevant tools
Familiarity with data visualisation tools such as Tableau, Power BI, or similar.
Experience with large datasets and data management systems & infrastructure.
Soft skills
Excellent project manager

You will be onsite in Montreal or remote.

HR Systems Support Analyst

The HR Systems Support Analyst role is an exciting opportunity to provide 1 st level human resources and user support for all global HR applications, focusing on Oracle Cloud HCM. Reporting to the Manager, HRIS, Compensation & Analytics, this role is an integral part of the Global Oracle Support Team and serves as a HR subject matter expert on content, processes and procedures providing operational support to internal stakeholders and end users.

Performance Expectations

 Providing superior customer service monitor, track and provide guidance to all global HR System users on policy/procedure questions and issues working to resolve inquiries and improve processes for an optimal user experience
 Identify technical system issues and work with the team to provide assistance in duplicating errors, troubleshooting and identifying root cause
 Support the rollout of annual HR programs as it pertains to HR Systems, such as compensation cycles, performance reviews, succession planning, etc.
 Assist with the creation of materials related to HR Systems procedures and policies (ex. work instructions, process documentation, FAQs, quick-reference cards etc.)
 Facilitate training for end users of HR Systems
 Assist in end to end system testing, including regression testing for new releases, user acceptance testing and issue duplication testing and documenting results
 Participate in Oracle HCM roadmap priorities, projects and implementations.
 Review and analyze the current system and identify opportunities for process and system enhancements either in existing designs or by adopting new functionalities and communicating a business case effectively
 Perform regular data integrity audits via reports and data manipulation ensuring all global sites are following processes and procedures.
 Assist in creating reports and extract data with the ability to manipulate and generate various ad-hoc reports using Oracle, Excel and PowerBI

Credentials

 Post-Secondary Education in Human Resources, Business Administration, Information Technology or related field.
 Working towards or in possession of CHRP or CHRL Designation is an asset.

Desired Characteristics

 3 years of progressive Human Resources systems support and analysis experience including hands on experience with HR applications
 Experience with Oracle Cloud Human Capital Management (HCM) a strong asset
 Strong understanding of HR processes and a keen interest in HR Systems design, structure, functions and processes
 Advanced proficiency with MS Office (Excel, Word, PowerPoint, Outlook) and working knowledge of HR policies and practices required.
 Highly analytical with the ability to assess current system design and make recommendations for improvement.
 Proven ability to adapt and work effectively in a variety of situations with changing or competing priorities
 Ability to work well in a Team environment that is highly collaborative
 A continuous improvement mindset and an exceptional customer service focus are critical for success along with exceptionally strong detail and problem-solving skills

 Opportunities for career advancement.

About the job
Affirm is reinventing credit to make it more honest and friendly, giving consumers the flexibility to buy now and pay later without any hidden fees or compounding interest.

We are seeking a highly skilled and experienced Senior Analyst to join our dynamic team, focusing on causal inference and the development of MVP versions of machine learning (ML) models. This role is pivotal in leveraging data science to understand the why behind our data, enabling informed decision-making and driving innovative solutions. The ideal candidate will have a strong background in statistical analysis, causal inference methodologies, and experience in building and iterating on ML models in a fast-paced environment.

What You Will Do

Causal Inference Analysis: Apply advanced causal inference techniques to uncover the underlying mechanisms and effects within our datasets, facilitating a deeper understanding of our data's drivers.
ML Modeling: Develop and refine MVP versions of ML models, focusing on rapid prototyping to test hypotheses and assess potential impact, with an eye towards scalability and integration into larger systems.
Cross-Functional Collaboration: Work closely with product, engineering, and business teams to define problem statements, identify data needs, and implement solutions that align with organizational goals.
Data Strategy Development: Contribute to the creation and execution of a comprehensive data strategy, emphasizing causal analysis and ML applications to support data-driven decision-making.
Insights Communication: Clearly communicate complex analytical findings and model outcomes to non-technical stakeholders, translating data insights into actionable business recommendations.

What We Look For

3+ years of experience in data analysis, with a strong focus on causal inference and ML modeling.
Proficiency in statistical software (R, Python) and familiarity with ML libraries (e.g., scikit-learn, TensorFlow).
Solid understanding of statistical modeling, experimental design, and A/B testing frameworks.
Exceptional analytical, problem-solving, and communication skills.
Bachelor's or Master's degree in Statistics, Computer Science, Economics, or a related quantitative field.

More About Hopper

At Hopper, we are on a mission to become the leading travel platform globally – powering Hopper’s mobile app, website and our B2B business, HTS (Hopper Technology Solutions). By leveraging massive amounts of data and advanced machine learning algorithms, Hopper combines its world-class travel agency offering with proprietary fintech products to bring transparency, flexibility and savings to travelers globally. We have developed several unique fintech solutions that address everything from pricing volatility to trip disruptions – helping people travel better and save more on their trips.

The Hopper platform serves hundreds of millions of travelers globally and continues to capture market share around the world. Ranked the third largest online travel agency in North America, the Hopper app has been downloaded over 120 million times and has become largely popular among younger travelers – with 70% of its users being Gen Z and millennials.

While everyone knows us as the Gen Z and Millennial travel app, Hopper has evolved to become much more than that. In recent years, we’ve grown into a global travel agency and travel fintech provider that powers some of the world’s largest brands.

Through HTS, our B2B division, the company supercharges its partners’ direct channels by integrating our fintech products on their sites or powering end-to-end travel portals. Today, our partners include leading travel brands like Capital One, Nubank, Air Canada and many more.

Here are just a few stats that demonstrate the company’s recent growth:

Hopper sells billion worth of travel and travel fintech every year. In 2023, over 1.3 billion trips were planned through the Hopper app and our HTS partnerships.

Our fintech products – including Price Freeze, Flexibility for Any Reason and Flight Disruption Assistance – have exceptionally strong CSAT because the terms are always clear, and customers receive instant, no-questions-asked resolutions.

Almost 30% of our app customers purchase at least one fintech product when making a booking; and consumers are 1.6x more likely to repurchase if they add fintech to their booking vs if they booked just travel.

Given the success of its fintech products, Hopper launched a B2B initiative, HTS (Hopper Technology Solutions), which represents more than 50% of the business.

Through HTS, any travel provider (airlines, hotels, banks, travel agencies, etc.) can integrate and seamlessly distribute Hopper’s fintech or travel inventory on their direct channels. As its first HTS partnership, the company partnered with Capital One to co-develop Capital One Travel, a new travel portal designed specifically for cardholders. Other HTS partners include Air Canada, Uber, CommBank, Nubank, Flair Airlines with many more in the pipeline.

Featured in Apple’s Best of the App Store list of Essential Travel Apps in 2023 and recognized by the likes of Fast Company’s Most Innovative Companies, Hopper has been downloaded over 120 million times and continues to have millions of new installs each month. Hopper is now the #3 largest online travel agency in North America and 70% of our app customers are Gen-Z and millennials travelers.

Hopper has raised over $750 million USD of private capital and is backed by some of the largest institutional investors and banks in the world. Hopper is primed to continue its acceleration as the world’s fastest-growing mobile-first travel marketplace.

Come take off with us!

Join our team

We live in and work in a rapidly evolving digital world where cyber security is critical. Protecting information and ensuring the reliability of network and services is paramount. The TELUS Health CSO team strives to always be steps ahead, tackling the toughest cyber security challenges head-on with top talent and cutting-edge technology.

The TELUS Health CSO team is committed to providing excellence in securing our internal and customers’ data and systems, ensuring world-class reliability of security networks and systems, and improving our overall cyber security posture. We manage our cyber risks and provide industry leading cyber governance, assurance and oversight to secure our data.

You’ll partner with other members of the CSO team to meet the cyber security needs of both TELUS Health and our customers in an increasingly complex and ever-changing cyber security landscape. We are passionate about learning and growing as individuals and as a team, all of which enables us to thrive in a dynamic, fast-paced environment.

Here's the impact you'll make and what we’ll accomplish together

As a Threat Intelligence Analyst, you will be an integral part of the TELUS Health Threat Intelligence team. Your primary role will be conducting collection and analysis, which you will leverage to produce various high-quality intelligence products. When doing so, you will use some of the latest and greatest tools and technologies to proactively identify and track emerging and existing threats to TELUS Health. By providing relevant, timely, and actionable reporting for stakeholders, you will help to effectively defend our organization and our customers against these threats. Together, we will improve the overall security posture of the organization by keeping everyone up to date and informed on the external threat landscape.

What your role will be


Be a part of global threat intelligence capability for TELUS Health as part of a wider CSO transformation programme.
Proactively identify and track threats to TELUS Health via the analysis of raw intelligence and data.
Conduct collection and analysis of information to produce high-quality intelligence products that are relevant, timely, and actionable by the wider TELUS Health CSO team.
Provide intelligence support to various CSO stakeholder initiatives, such as training or special projects.

Business Data Stewardship

Monitors and evaluates data governance effectiveness, identifying opportunities for improvement and driving necessary changes.

More About Hopper

At Hopper, we are on a mission to become the leading travel platform globally – powering Hopper’s mobile app, website and our B2B business, HTS (Hopper Technology Solutions). By leveraging massive amounts of data and advanced machine learning algorithms, Hopper combines its world-class travel agency offering with proprietary fintech products to bring transparency, flexibility and savings to travelers globally. We have developed several unique fintech solutions that address everything from pricing volatility to trip disruptions – helping people travel better and save more on their trips.

The Hopper platform serves hundreds of millions of travelers globally and continues to capture market share around the world. Ranked the third largest online travel agency in North America, the Hopper app has been downloaded over 120 million times and has become largely popular among younger travelers – with 70% of its users being Gen Z and millennials.

While everyone knows us as the Gen Z and Millennial travel app, Hopper has evolved to become much more than that. In recent years, we’ve grown into a global travel agency and travel fintech provider that powers some of the world’s largest brands.

Through HTS, our B2B division, the company supercharges its partners’ direct channels by integrating our fintech products on their sites or powering end-to-end travel portals. Today, our partners include leading travel brands like Capital One, Nubank, Air Canada and many more.

Here are just a few stats that demonstrate the company’s recent growth:

Hopper sells billion worth of travel and travel fintech every year. In 2023, over 1.3 billion trips were planned through the Hopper app and our HTS partnerships.

Our fintech products – including Price Freeze, Flexibility for Any Reason and Flight Disruption Assistance – have exceptionally strong CSAT because the terms are always clear, and customers receive instant, no-questions-asked resolutions.

Almost 30% of our app customers purchase at least one fintech product when making a booking; and consumers are 1.6x more likely to repurchase if they add fintech to their booking vs if they booked just travel.

Given the success of its fintech products, Hopper launched a B2B initiative, HTS (Hopper Technology Solutions), which represents more than 50% of the business.

Through HTS, any travel provider (airlines, hotels, banks, travel agencies, etc.) can integrate and seamlessly distribute Hopper’s fintech or travel inventory on their direct channels. As its first HTS partnership, the company partnered with Capital One to co-develop Capital One Travel, a new travel portal designed specifically for cardholders. Other HTS partners include Air Canada, Uber, CommBank, Nubank, Flair Airlines with many more in the pipeline.

Featured in Apple’s Best of the App Store list of Essential Travel Apps in 2023 and recognized by the likes of Fast Company’s Most Innovative Companies, Hopper has been downloaded over 120 million times and continues to have millions of new installs each month. Hopper is now the #3 largest online travel agency in North America and 70% of our app customers are Gen-Z and millennials travelers.

Hopper has raised over $750 million USD of private capital and is backed by some of the largest institutional investors and banks in the world. Hopper is primed to continue its acceleration as the world’s fastest-growing mobile-first travel marketplace.

Come take off with us!

About the job
Are you a Master’s prepared registered nurse interested and experienced in research? Are you passionate about evidence-based practice and leading change? Do you enjoy facilitating discussions and working within a highly skilled team? This may be the role for you!

JOB SUMMARY:
The Guideline Development Methodologist (GDM) is a Master’s prepared registered nurse responsible for leading the planning, research and execution of best practice guidelines (BPG). The GDM will support the work of an interprofessional expert panel by: conducting systematic reviews of the literature; developing evidence-based recommendation statements; writing the guideline, reports and manuscripts for peer-review; and prepare and present research for scientific meetings. The GDM works collaboratively with RNAOs Implementation Science and Evaluation/Monitoring Teams to support implementation, evaluation and sustainability of evidence-based practice cultures.

As a GDM you will work on guidelines across a wide range of topics, including: clinical, foundational, health equity, healthy work environment, and others. As a member of the guideline development team, you will be assigned to other best practice guideline development initiatives as well.

RESPONSIBILITIES:
work collaboratively with members of the Research Team, other IABPG team members (Implementation Science and Evaluation/Monitoring team), Expert Panel members, health sciences librarians, and other subject matter experts to develop, facilitate, and maintain methodological rigour, clinical significance, and completion timelines for BPGs
plan and conduct systematic reviews of defined research questions, including rapid and comprehensive literature searches, literature screening and relevance reviews, data extraction, quality appraisal, and evidence synthesis to identify valid and applicable evidence for RNAO best practice guidelines and other RNAO initiatives
contribute to the rigour of the guideline development process to maintain international standards. Specifically use Grading of Recommendations Assessment, Development and Evaluation (GRADE and GRADE CERQual) to quality appraise evidence and develop evidence to decision frameworks
lead activities related to the systematic review process, including locating, retrieving, filing, and distributing research reports
produce search results, data extraction, evidence profiles, evidence to decision, and work updates for review by the Director, Associate Director, Senior Manager and Expert Panel members as requiredoversee and direct the BPG development process for assigned BPGs from identifying key issues in the proposed guideline area of focus to final publication of the BPG including:
take the lead role in identifying and recommending a representative panel of experts
lead the systematic review process, as noted above
develop draft evidence-based recommendations for best practice guidelines
lead consensus-building process with expert panels to finalize evidence-based recommendations including content, context and their strength
draft complete guidelines for expert panel review within completion timeframes.
edit, review and refine guidelines based upon expert panel and internal/external stakeholder feedback within completion timeframes
prepare the best practice guidelines documents, writing and editing, both drafts and final documents and other documents as required
support the development of performance indicators for the BPG and when appropriate for Nursing Quality Indicators for Reporting & Evaluation® (NQuIRE)
be a champion for current and emerging evidence development and review and guideline development methodology supporting evidence-based nursing practice
draft and prepare manuscripts for publication
mentor and train other staff as required
SKILL, KNOWLEDGE AND EXPERIENCE:
registered nurse with in-depth, demonstrated understanding of evidence-based nursing practice.
current registration in good standing with the College of Nurses of Ontario and in RNAO.
master’s degree in nursing, health research or a related field is required, or equivalent combination of preparation and experience (Thesis prepared preferred).
three to five years research experience and clinical nursing experience.
in-depth knowledge of systematic review methodology.
strong interest or experience in nursing best practice guideline development.
superior organizational skills and self-directed work ethic to effectively manage multiple projects in various stages of development.
high flexibility and adaptability in responding to new research opportunities as they arise.
excellent analytical skills and detail-orientation.
excellent written and verbal communication and interpersonal skills to deal effectively with staff and stakeholders, to synthesize and present information, to prepare manuscripts and to conduct the research work.
strong experience with citation management software (such as Reference Manager, RefWorks, or EndNote) and online biomedical and allied health bibliographic databases (such as Medline, CINAHL, or Embase).
dexterity required to operate a computer, telephone, and other office equipment.
EFFORT:
Continuous concentration is required to read, screen, and appraise a large volume of information daily, prepare data tables and summary reports, and to consult as appropriate.
Sight, touch and hearing are used to read, proofread, write, and analyze information and to answer enquiries.
Sitting is required frequently in the job for more than 2 hours at a time to read and write information, work on the computer, participate in virtual/inperson meetings.
Workflow requires re-prioritizing of workload, meeting multiple demands, and working overtime as required.
WORKING CONDITIONS:
works in a climate-controlled office with some exposure to distractions, interruptions and stress from multiple demands.
typical conditions are such that no risk or injury is present.

Quantitative Analyst, Portfolio Analytics

OMERS Total Portfolio Management manages the public markets investment portfolio consisting of fixed income (including government bonds, Inflation-Linked Bonds and public and private credit) and equities, including global public equities, intellectual property and structured investments. The team’s approach is focused on generating current income from high-quality assets and generating a consistent capital return with a lower volatility than the broad markets. We also seek to develop strategic partnerships with best-in-class investors to access credit and other opportunities on a global basis. The OMERS Capital Markets' team is distinguished by its diversity in expertise and experience and its commitment to reliable, lower-risk performance. Our objective is to construct a well-diversified portfolio that will deliver long-term annualized returns in the 6 to 9% range.

Job Description

As a member of the OMERS Total Portfolio Management (TPM) team in Toronto, reporting to the Director, Head of Portfolio Analytics, you will contribute and lead our transformation of how Capital Markets improves investment decision making through data driven insights.

The role provides the successful candidate with the opportunity to work closely with the Global Credit team, where you will develop and grow your understanding of quantitative and technical tools that drive the development of the systematic components of portfolio management.

Conduct innovative tech, data, and investment research to deliver impactful analytics and insights to Capital Market investment team

Our story

Founded in 1962, OMERS is one of Canada’s largest defined benefit pension plans, with $127.4 billion in net assets as at June 30, 2023. OMERS is a jointly-sponsored pension plan, with more than 1,000 participating employers ranging from large cities to local agencies, and over half a million active, deferred and retired members. OMERS members include union and non-union employees of municipalities, school boards, local boards, transit systems, electrical utilities, emergency services and children’s aid societies across Ontario. Contributions to the Plan are funded equally by members and employers. OMERS teams work in Toronto, London, New York, Amsterdam, Luxembourg, Singapore, Sydney and other major cities across North America and Europe – serving members and employers and originating and managing a diversified portfolio of high-quality investments in public markets, private equity, infrastructure and real estate.

OMERS is committed to having a workforce that reflects the communities in which we live and work. We are an equal opportunity employer committed to a barrier-free recruitment and selection process. At OMERS inclusion and diversity means belonging. How we create a sense of belonging is through our employees and our vast network of Employee Resource Groups. Whether you are passionate about gender, pride, or visible minorities, we have groups that are focused on making a difference in all of our lives.

Who You'll Work With

You will report to the Senior Manager, Risk & Performance Analytics and work with a team of passionate professionals to constantly challenge status quo and improve the portfolio and risk reporting and attribution practices at OTPP. What You'll Do

Ensure that data for the total fund and risk system is collected, input, and validated in an efficient manner and any issues arising from the processes are either resolved or escalated as required
Calculate and generate portfolio exposure reporting at total fund level, including but not limited to the fund’s asset mix, currency mix, country exposure, liquidity and leverage risk etc at portfolio and total fund level
Produce counterparty risk reports across business line and at total fund level and conduct factor and trade attribution analysis on material day over day exposure and VaR movements

Perform credit monitoring of OTPP’s counterparties
Monitor investment exposure and risk usage against board investment policy limit and escalate as required
Maintain and enhance the business intelligence reporting suite and various analysis tools developed in-house to facilitate deeper understanding of portfolio and risk movement
Supporting the development and testing of risk model enhancements and reporting improvements

About the job
Affirm is reinventing credit to make it more honest and friendly, giving consumers the flexibility to buy now and pay later without any hidden fees or compounding interest.

We are seeking a highly skilled and experienced Senior Analyst to join our dynamic team, focusing on causal inference and the development of MVP versions of machine learning (ML) models. This role is pivotal in leveraging data science to understand the why behind our data, enabling informed decision-making and driving innovative solutions. The ideal candidate will have a strong background in statistical analysis, causal inference methodologies, and experience in building and iterating on ML models in a fast-paced environment.

What You Will Do

Causal Inference Analysis: Apply advanced causal inference techniques to uncover the underlying mechanisms and effects within our datasets, facilitating a deeper understanding of our data's drivers.
ML Modeling: Develop and refine MVP versions of ML models, focusing on rapid prototyping to test hypotheses and assess potential impact, with an eye towards scalability and integration into larger systems.
Cross-Functional Collaboration: Work closely with product, engineering, and business teams to define problem statements, identify data needs, and implement solutions that align with organizational goals.
Data Strategy Development: Contribute to the creation and execution of a comprehensive data strategy, emphasizing causal analysis and ML applications to support data-driven decision-making.
Insights Communication: Clearly communicate complex analytical findings and model outcomes to non-technical stakeholders, translating data insights into actionable business recommendations.

What We Look For

3+ years of experience in data analysis, with a strong focus on causal inference and ML modeling.
Proficiency in statistical software (R, Python) and familiarity with ML libraries (e.g., scikit-learn, TensorFlow).
Solid understanding of statistical modeling, experimental design, and A/B testing frameworks.
Exceptional analytical, problem-solving, and communication skills.
Bachelor's or Master's degree in Statistics, Computer Science, Economics, or a related quantitative field.

À propos du poste:

Relevant du responsable des services transactionnels régionaux pour le processus d’approvisionnement au paiement (P2P), vous serez responsable de la gouvernance, des indicateurs de rendement clés, de la production de rapports et des processus opérationnels.
Le spécialiste en gouvernance et rapports joue un rôle de facilitateur et de catalyseur en veillant à ce que les processus de gouvernance favorisent la transparence, la responsabilité et une prise de décision efficace au sein du groupe des services transactionnels pour le processus d’approvisionnement au paiement (P2P).
Élaborer et tenir à jour des indicateurs de rendement clés et des rapports connexes concernant les processus d’approvisionnement au paiement (P2P) et les données sur le rendement, les mesures et les tendances connexes au sein de la fonction des services transactionnels, à des fins d’information et de prise de décision pour la direction et les parties prenantes.


Plus spécifiquement, vous aurez à:


Organiser des réunions en élaborant des ordres du jour, en préparant et en rassemblant les documents nécessaires, et en assurant la liaison avec les parties prenantes en vue de leur implication.
Diriger les discussions des réunions de gouvernance en respectant les ordres du jour, en guidant la prise de décision et en favorisant le consensus, afin d’obtenir des résultats productifs pour l’équipe.
Rédiger les procès-verbaux, les décisions et les plans d’action pour référence ultérieure, en veillant à ce que les résultats des réunions, les décisions et les mesures à prendre soient communiqués en temps utile aux parties prenantes concernées.
Offrir des conseils, des ateliers ou des séances de formation sur les principes et les pratiques de gouvernance aux membres de l’équipe.
Évaluer l’efficience et l’efficacité de la structure de gouvernance et recommander des améliorations.
Identifier les possibilités d’amélioration des processus dans le cadre de la gouvernance.
Produire des rapports sur les indicateurs de rendement clés afin de garantir l’exactitude de l’extraction et de la fonctionnalité des données, en vue de soutenir les cycles de rapports financiers.
Recueillir des données quantitatives à partir de plateformes telles que SAP afin de créer des rapports cohérents et précis sur les processus d’approvisionnement au paiement (P2P).
Élaborer et tenir à jour des rapports sur les indicateurs de rendement clés qui reflètent l’aspect financier et de performance des processus d’approvisionnement au paiement (P2P) en respectant les exigences en matière de conformité et de processus internes.


Compétences:


Baccalauréat ou maîtrise dans un domaine pertinent tel que comptabilité, finances, gestion des opérations ou gestion de la chaîne d’approvisionnement.
Plus de cinq ans d’expérience dans un rôle similaire avec une maîtrise des plateformes SAP et Power BI. Expérience avec la plateforme Coupa Procure-to-Pay, un atout.
Volonté de se tenir au courant des meilleures pratiques et des technologies émergentes.
Capacité à analyser des données, à identifier des tendances et à extraire des informations significatives pour éclairer la prise de décision en mettant l’accent sur l’obtention de résultats.
Maîtrise de l’élaboration et de la mise à jour de rapports, de tableaux de bord et d’indicateurs de rendement clés (IRC) en vue d’une communication efficace des mesures de performance.
Compréhension des principes de gouvernance et des normes de conformité.



Langues : Français et anglais (maîtrise obligatoire)


Voyage : Des déplacements régionaux et dans le monde entier peuvent être nécessaires.


Ce que nous offrons:



Culture professionnelle favorisant la sécurité, l’intégrité, la responsabilité, l’ouverture d’esprit, la simplicité et l’entrepreneuriat
Régime d’avantages sociaux concurrentiel et complet
Horaires de travail souples
Programmes de mieux être des employés
Perspectives de développement professionnel


Le genre masculin est utilisé sans discrimination, pour alléger le texte.

La priorité sera donnée aux candidats ayant le droit de travailler au Canada.
Glencore est un employeur qui respecte l’équité en matière d’emploi et qui s’engage à créer et à maintenir une main-d’œuvre diversifiée. Si vous avez besoin de mesures d’adaptation dans le processus de sélection, veuillez-nous le faire savoir par courriel à talentacquisitioncopper@glencore.ca.

Location: Laval, Quebec
Job type: Permanent full-time position

About Glencore:

Glencore is one of the world’s largest diversified natural resources companies. It is also a major producer and marketer of more than 60 commodities. Our operations include approximately 150 mining and metallurgical sites and agricultural oil facilities supported by a global network. Our mission is to provide the commodities that make everyday life better, in a socially responsible way. Our people are fundamental to our success. We employ some 135,000 people and offer them the opportunity to develop and grow their skills and careers.

About the role:

Reporting to the Regions Procure-To-Pay (P2P) Transactional Services Leader, you will be responsible for governance, KPIs, reporting and business processes.
The Governance and Reporting specialist acts as a facilitator and enabler, ensuring that the governance processes promote transparency, accountability, and effective decision-making within the P2P transactional services group.
Develop and maintain KPI and related reports relating to P2P processes and related performance data, metrics, and trends within the transactional services function for management and stakeholder information and decision-making purposes.

More specifically, you will:

 Orchestrate meetings by developing agendas, preparing, and assembling necessary documents, and liaising with stakeholders for their engagement.
 Lead governance meeting discussions aligned with agendas, guiding decision-making, and fostering consensus, driving productive outcomes for the team.
Record meeting minutes, decisions, and action plans for future reference, ensuring timely sharing of meeting outcomes, decisions, and action items with relevant stakeholders.
Offer guidance, workshops, or training sessions on governance principles and practices for team members.
Assess the efficiency and efficacy of governance structure and recommend improvements.
Identify areas for process enhancement within the governance framework.
Operate within KPI reporting frameworks to ensure accurate data extraction and functionality, supporting financial reporting cycles.
Gather quantitative data from enterprise systems like SAP to create consistent and accurate reports for P2P (Procure-to-Pay) processes.
Develop and maintain KPI reports reflecting P2P financials and related performance, meeting compliance and internal process requirements.
Review and amend reports as needed to meet evolving circumstances and stakeholder requirements.



Skills:

A bachelor’s or master’s degree in a relevant field such as accounting, finance, operations management, or supply chain management.
5+ years in a similar role with proficiency in SAP, Power BI. Experience in Coupa Procure-to-Pay Platform environment is an advantage.
Willingness to stay updated on best practices and emerging technologies.
Ability to analyze data, identify trends, and extract meaningful insights to inform decision-making with a focus on achieving results.
Proficiency in developing and maintaining reports, dashboards, and key performance indicators (KPIs) for effective communication of performance metrics.
Understanding of governance principles and compliance standards.
Adept at identifying issues, proposing solutions, and implementing improvements to enhance governance and reporting processes.





Languages: French and English (Fluency is Mandatory)

Travel: Within the region and globally may be required.

What we offer:
A work culture that promotes safety, integrity, responsibility, open-mindedness, simplicity, and entrepreneurship.
A competitive, comprehensive benefits plan.
Flexible working hours.
Employee wellness programs.
Professional development opportunities.

The masculine gender is used, without discrimination, to lighten the text.

Priority will be given to candidates with the right to work in Canada.

About the job
Affirm is reinventing credit to make it more honest and friendly, giving consumers the flexibility to buy now and pay later without any hidden fees or compounding interest.

We are seeking a highly skilled and experienced Senior Analyst to join our dynamic team, focusing on causal inference and the development of MVP versions of machine learning (ML) models. This role is pivotal in leveraging data science to understand the why behind our data, enabling informed decision-making and driving innovative solutions. The ideal candidate will have a strong background in statistical analysis, causal inference methodologies, and experience in building and iterating on ML models in a fast-paced environment.

What You Will Do

Causal Inference Analysis: Apply advanced causal inference techniques to uncover the underlying mechanisms and effects within our datasets, facilitating a deeper understanding of our data's drivers.
ML Modeling: Develop and refine MVP versions of ML models, focusing on rapid prototyping to test hypotheses and assess potential impact, with an eye towards scalability and integration into larger systems.
Cross-Functional Collaboration: Work closely with product, engineering, and business teams to define problem statements, identify data needs, and implement solutions that align with organizational goals.
Data Strategy Development: Contribute to the creation and execution of a comprehensive data strategy, emphasizing causal analysis and ML applications to support data-driven decision-making.
Insights Communication: Clearly communicate complex analytical findings and model outcomes to non-technical stakeholders, translating data insights into actionable business recommendations.

What We Look For

3+ years of experience in data analysis, with a strong focus on causal inference and ML modeling.
Proficiency in statistical software (R, Python) and familiarity with ML libraries (e.g., scikit-learn, TensorFlow).
Solid understanding of statistical modeling, experimental design, and A/B testing frameworks.
Exceptional analytical, problem-solving, and communication skills.
Bachelor's or Master's degree in Statistics, Computer Science, Economics, or a related quantitative field.

About the job
Principal level position in Biostatistics with job responsibilities that include but are not limited to the following:

Responsible for protocol development including study design, sample size calculation, randomization, and statistical analysis plan for assigned studies.
Provide statistical oversight to studies and assure adequate quality and consistency with project requirements.
Responsible for assuring that data for statistical analyses are complete, accurate and consistent.
Responsible for statistical analysis plans and the accuracy and timeliness of statistical input into reports or decisions.
Responsible for validity of analysis and explore alternative analysis strategies as needed.
Demonstrates extensive understanding of statistical concepts and methodologies. Recognizes and corrects flaws in scientific reasoning and statistical interpretation.
Responsible for accuracy and consistency of statistical tables, figures, and data listings, accuracy of report text, and consistency between summary tables in the body of reports and the corresponding source tables and listings.
Responsible for statistical methods section for the reports. Identifies and corrects common flaws in interpretation of results, inconsistency in presentation or inference, adherence to the report guidelines, and assures project-wide consistency.
Effectively mentor peers with regards to statistical methodology and provide appropriate training to less experienced statisticians.
Manage activities of statisticians across projects by appropriately coordinating assignments and reviewing work so that projects are delivered on time with high quality.


Requirements:

MS or PhD in Statistics, Biostatistics or related field. PhD with 3-5 years of experience or MS with 6-8 years of experience.
Strong oral and written communications skills, with ability to effectively communicate internally and with clients.
Demonstrated understanding and insight in statistics, drug development process and relevant FDA regulations.
Pharmaceutical, CRO, or related industry experience with clinical trials, including interaction with Regulatory Agencies, especially FDA.

About the job
About Agoda

Agoda is an online travel booking platform for accommodations, flights, and more. We build and deploy cutting-edge technology that connects travelers with more than 3.6 million accommodations globally. Based in Asia and part of Booking Holdings, our 6,000+ employees representing 90+ nationalities foster a work environment rich in diversity, creativity, and collaboration. We innovate through a culture of experimentation and ownership, enhancing the ability for our customers to experience the world.

 Get to Know our  Team: 

The Flights Marketing Team of Agoda is a world leader in online marketing. This department is highly data-driven and focused on developing at-scale marketing programs that improve the lifetime value of Agoda customers through measurable marketing programs and channels. The team is a blend of the best analysts, marketing strategists, and data scientists in the world. The marketing leadership at Agoda have deep experience in data science, product, strategy, and other marketing fields and have built an organization that thrives on data, creative ideas, and technology. The Performance Marketing – Flight Team also fosters a great learning environment. You will be able to learn and grow by working closely with experts from a variety of backgrounds from all over the world.

 In this Role, you’ll get  to: 

You’ll be heavily involved in growing our Flights business
Experiment with various pricing strategies on Agoda and Metasearch to grow the business
Analyze massive amounts of data generated in experiments, build dashboards, and develop predictive models
Work with diverse stakeholders to arrive at investment plans for markets and channels

 What you’ll Need to  Succeed: 

Bachelor’s Degree or higher from top university in a quantitative subject (computer science, mathematics, engineering, statistics or science)
Ability to communicate fluently and succinctly in English 
Good numerical reasoning skills
Strong problem solving skills
Proficiency in Excel and SQL
Intellectual curiosity

 It’s Great if you  Have: 

Exposure to one or more data analysis packages or databases, e.g., SAS, R, SPSS, Python, VBA, SQL
Experience in digital marketing

About the job
Vous jouerez un rôle essentiel dans la résolution des problèmes de données et d'ingénierie visant à améliorer les offres d'hébergement de Hopper, faisant de Hopper le meilleur endroit pour réserver des hôtels et des locations de vacances.

Ce rôle a un impact énorme sur la vision et le succès de l'entreprise. C'est une occasion unique de rejoindre l'une des équipes stratégiques d'hébergement de Hopper et d'avoir accès à des ensembles de données fascinantes et massives sur le marché et les comportements.

Votre principale responsabilité consistera à prendre en charge l'entreposage de nos données, à garantir l'accessibilité des données et à fournir des informations qui façonneront notre orientation stratégique.

Il s'agit d'une formidable occasion de croissance personnelle et comprend un potentiel élevé d'avantages sur les options d'achat d'actions avant l'introduction en bourse.

Ta routine ressemblerait à quoi?

Vous assurer que ces pipelines sont robustes, efficaces et constamment mis à jour pour fournir des informations en temps réel.
Propriété de l'entrepôt de données : Assumer pleinement la responsabilité de notre entrepôt de données, en en faisant une ressource accessible et conviviale pour les équipes de produits et les équipes commerciales. Indicateurs de performance clés et cadres d'établissement de rapports : identifier, affiner et suivre les indicateurs de performance clés (KPI) essentiels à l'évaluation de la performance de l'entreprise. Élaborer et maintenir des cadres de rapports qui permettent un suivi et des rapports continus de ces mesures.
Rapports de base pour la prise de décision : créer et gérer des systèmes de rapports de base qui pilotent à la fois les décisions opérationnelles quotidiennes et les décisions stratégiques à long terme. Veiller à ce que ces rapports fournissent des informations exploitables et soient facilement accessibles aux parties prenantes concernées.
Possibilités de croissance des revenus : en devenant un expert de nos données et en comprenant parfaitement nos clients, identifier de manière proactive de nouvelles possibilités de croissance des revenus. Collaborer avec des équipes transversales pour mettre en œuvre des stratégies qui capitalisent sur ces possibilités.
Autonomie dans la résolution de problèmes : identifier les défis liés aux données et développer des solutions créatives de manière indépendante. Démontrer une approche proactive en matière de résolution de problèmes et un engagement envers la qualité et l'exactitude des données.

More About Hopper

At Hopper, we are on a mission to become the leading travel platform globally – powering Hopper’s mobile app, website and our B2B business, HTS (Hopper Technology Solutions). By leveraging massive amounts of data and advanced machine learning algorithms, Hopper combines its world-class travel agency offering with proprietary fintech products to bring transparency, flexibility and savings to travelers globally. We have developed several unique fintech solutions that address everything from pricing volatility to trip disruptions – helping people travel better and save more on their trips.

The Hopper platform serves hundreds of millions of travelers globally and continues to capture market share around the world. Ranked the third largest online travel agency in North America, the Hopper app has been downloaded over 120 million times and has become largely popular among younger travelers – with 70% of its users being Gen Z and millennials.

While everyone knows us as the Gen Z and Millennial travel app, Hopper has evolved to become much more than that. In recent years, we’ve grown into a global travel agency and travel fintech provider that powers some of the world’s largest brands.

Through HTS, our B2B division, the company supercharges its partners’ direct channels by integrating our fintech products on their sites or powering end-to-end travel portals. Today, our partners include leading travel brands like Capital One, Nubank, Air Canada and many more.

Here are just a few stats that demonstrate the company’s recent growth:

Hopper sells billion worth of travel and travel fintech every year. In 2023, over 1.3 billion trips were planned through the Hopper app and our HTS partnerships.

Our fintech products – including Price Freeze, Flexibility for Any Reason and Flight Disruption Assistance – have exceptionally strong CSAT because the terms are always clear, and customers receive instant, no-questions-asked resolutions.

Almost 30% of our app customers purchase at least one fintech product when making a booking; and consumers are 1.6x more likely to repurchase if they add fintech to their booking vs if they booked just travel.

Given the success of its fintech products, Hopper launched a B2B initiative, HTS (Hopper Technology Solutions), which represents more than 50% of the business.

Through HTS, any travel provider (airlines, hotels, banks, travel agencies, etc.) can integrate and seamlessly distribute Hopper’s fintech or travel inventory on their direct channels. As its first HTS partnership, the company partnered with Capital One to co-develop Capital One Travel, a new travel portal designed specifically for cardholders. Other HTS partners include Air Canada, Uber, CommBank, Nubank, Flair Airlines with many more in the pipeline.

Featured in Apple’s Best of the App Store list of Essential Travel Apps in 2023 and recognized by the likes of Fast Company’s Most Innovative Companies, Hopper has been downloaded over 120 million times and continues to have millions of new installs each month. Hopper is now the #3 largest online travel agency in North America and 70% of our app customers are Gen-Z and millennials travelers.

Hopper has raised over $750 million USD of private capital and is backed by some of the largest institutional investors and banks in the world. Hopper is primed to continue its acceleration as the world’s fastest-growing mobile-first travel marketplace.

Come take off with us!

Affirm is reinventing credit to make it more honest and friendly, giving consumers the flexibility to buy now and pay later without any hidden fees or compounding interest.

We are seeking a highly skilled and experienced Senior Analyst to join our dynamic team, focusing on causal inference and the development of MVP versions of machine learning (ML) models. This role is pivotal in leveraging data science to understand the why behind our data, enabling informed decision-making and driving innovative solutions. The ideal candidate will have a strong background in statistical analysis, causal inference methodologies, and experience in building and iterating on ML models in a fast-paced environment.

What You Will Do

Causal Inference Analysis: Apply advanced causal inference techniques to uncover the underlying mechanisms and effects within our datasets, facilitating a deeper understanding of our data's drivers.
ML Modeling: Develop and refine MVP versions of ML models, focusing on rapid prototyping to test hypotheses and assess potential impact, with an eye towards scalability and integration into larger systems.
Cross-Functional Collaboration: Work closely with product, engineering, and business teams to define problem statements, identify data needs, and implement solutions that align with organizational goals.
Data Strategy Development: Contribute to the creation and execution of a comprehensive data strategy, emphasizing causal analysis and ML applications to support data-driven decision-making.
Insights Communication: Clearly communicate complex analytical findings and model outcomes to non-technical stakeholders, translating data insights into actionable business recommendations.

What We Look For

3+ years of experience in data analysis, with a strong focus on causal inference and ML modeling.
Proficiency in statistical software (R, Python) and familiarity with ML libraries (e.g., scikit-learn, TensorFlow).
Solid understanding of statistical modeling, experimental design, and A/B testing frameworks.
Exceptional analytical, problem-solving, and communication skills.
Bachelor's or Master's degree in Statistics, Computer Science, Economics, or a related quantitative field.

Programmeur Analyste Business Intelligence (BI)
Notre organisation est activement à la recherche d'un Programmeur Analyste en Business Intelligence (BI), qui occupera une position centrale dans nos efforts visant à développer et à enrichir notre plateforme d'intelligence d'affaires. Au sein de notre entreprise, la pratique BI bénéficie d'un soutien institutionnel fort, incarné par une équipe entièrement dédiée d'analystes d'affaires BI, témoignant de notre engagement envers l'excellence dans ce domaine.
Le candidat sélectionné jouera un rôle déterminant en soutenant l'organisation dans le développement de notre architecture de données et aussi en orchestrant la transformation des données issues de diverses sources. Ceci est crucial pour nous permettre de tirer des insights précis et d'optimiser nos processus décisionnels. En outre, le candidat retenu sera chargé des responsabilités suivantes :
Concevoir des modèles pour les entrepôts de données en alignement avec les exigences spécifiées par les analystes pour l'exploitation des données, garantissant ainsi une réponse efficace aux besoins d'analyse.
Examiner et affiner l'architecture des processus de transformation des données pour améliorer leur performance et efficacité, visant une optimisation systématique de l'exécution.
Collaborer étroitement avec les équipes d'analystes pour définir avec précision les spécifications des interfaces utilisateurs et des rapports analytiques, assurant une adéquation parfaite avec les besoins métier.
Participer activement à la planification, à la conception et au développement de solutions ETL robustes, facilitant le transfert et l'intégration des données depuis divers systèmes opérationnels vers les entrepôts de données et data lakes.
Élaborer et tenir à jour une documentation technique détaillée pour chaque développement, favorisant ainsi une compréhension et une maintenance efficaces des systèmes.
Conduire des tests unitaires d'intégration pour garantir la fiabilité et la qualité des développements avant leur déploiement.
Fournir un support technique fiable lors du lancement de nouveaux développements, assurant une transition sans heurts vers la production.
S'engager dans un processus continu d'apprentissage et de perfectionnement des compétences techniques, en se tenant au courant des dernières innovations et pratiques technologiques.
Mener des analyses approfondies pour diagnostiquer et corriger les incidents, ainsi que pour supporter l'évolution des solutions BI en place.
Prendre en charge des initiatives de gestion des données, incluant la préparation, la modélisation, le profilage et le nettoyage des données, afin d'assurer leur qualité et leur intégrité.
Concevoir et maintenir des outils de scripts pour l'automatisation et la synchronisation, ainsi que des processus d'extraction et de chargement des données, améliorant l'efficacité et la fluidité du traitement des données.

DEC ou Bachelier en informatique de gestion, génie ou toute combinaison de formation et d’expérience pertinente

Expérience en modélisation d’entrepôts données et bases de données relationnelles
Expérience en développement ETL de rapports et tableau de bord (SSIS, SSRS, PowerBI, SQL , Power Query)
Expertise en construction d’interfaces et en échange de données (JSON, XML, CSV, API)
Expertise avec Microsoft Data Factory et Synapse
Expertise en résolution de problèmes complexes, incluant des problèmes de performances

TD Description

Our Values

At TD we're guided by our purpose is to enrich the lives of our customers, communities and colleagues, and share a set of values that shape our culture and guide our behavior. In exchange for how our colleagues show up to help TD succeed, we are committed to delivering a colleague experience grounded in Impact, Growth and a Culture of Care. No matter where you work across TD, we empower you to make an impact at work and in your community, explore and grow your career and be part of our caring and inclusive culture.



A supportive culture that promotes colleague well-being is core to who we are. At TD, we focus on total well-being with extensive programs to help colleagues assess, manage, and improve their well-being across four core pillars — physical, financial, social and mental/emotional. In addition, we champion a safe and inclusive work environment so colleagues feel a sense of belonging and feel supported in their personal and professional growth. Through our focus on well-being, we know that we can help our colleagues thrive, contribute to our culture of care, and support better business outcomes, because when colleagues feel their best, they're more likely to do their best.



Our Total Rewards package reflects the investment we make in our colleagues to help them, and their families achieve their well-being goals. Total Rewards at TD includes a base salary, variable compensation, and several other key plans such as health and well-being benefits including medical, dental, vision & mental health coverage, savings and retirement programs, paid time off, banking benefits and discounts, career development, and reward and recognition programs.



At TD, we believe in-person connections fuel collaboration and collective creativity. Our workplace experience empowers colleagues to do great work side-by-side at TD locations, while offering flexibility to work remotely where it makes sense for the work and team. Our teams work in one of three workplace models: Hybrid, Onsite and Primarily Remote. Wherever our colleagues are working, they’ll always have access to the TD community and experience our culture of care.



TD is one of the world's leading global financial institutions and is the fifth largest bank in North America by branches. Every day, we deliver legendary customer experiences to over 27 million households and businesses in Canada, the United States and around the world. More than 95,000 TD colleagues bring their skills, talent, and creativity to the Bank, those we serve, and the economies we support. We are guided by our vision to Be the Better Bank and our purpose to enrich the lives of our customers, communities and colleagues.

TD is deeply committed to being a leader in customer experience, that is why we believe that all colleagues, no matter where they work, are customer facing. As we build our business and deliver on our strategy, we are innovating to enhance the customer experience and build capabilities to shape the future of banking. Whether you’ve got years of banking experience or are just starting your career in financial services, we can help you realize your potential. Through regular leadership and development conversations to mentorship and training programs, we’re here to support you towards your goals. As an organization, we keep growing – and so will you.



We can't afford to be boring. Neither can you. The scale and scope of what TD does may surprise you. The rapid pace of change makes it a business imperative for us to be smart and open-minded in the way we think about strategy. TD's strategy and business teams become more intertwined as new opportunities present themselves. This new era in banking does not equal boring. Not at TD, Not at Risk, Not at Fraud strategy, anyway.

The Fraud Risk Management & Global Security and Investigations (FRM & GSI) is an enterprise-level body that strives to protect TD Bank Group customers, shareholders and employees from financial crimes and fraud. Aligned with TD strategy and risk appetite, FRM & GSI develops and evolves enterprise policies, advanced analytics capabilities and operational processes to improve governance, oversight, and collaboration between fraud management and other control functions within the Bank.

The Canadian Fraud Management (CFM) team operates within FRM & GSI in a fast-paced environment requiring both strategic and tactical responses to changing fraud patterns and provides a unique opportunity to apply critical thinking and leadership skills in an innovation centric environmenWe can't afford to be boring.
